 <text xml:lang="sa-Latn">
  <body>

   <div n="1" type="sthāna">

    <head xml:lang="en">[Sūtrasthāna 32-end]</head>

    <div n="32" type="adhyāya">
     
     <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 32, draft based on MS H]</head>



     <l xml:id="SS.1.32.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.32.1</label>
       athātaḥ svabhāvavipratipattiṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.32.2"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.32.3-4"><label>1931 ed. 1.32.3-4</label>
       svabhāvaprasiddhānāṃ śarīraikadeśānām anyathātvaṃ maraṇāya | tad yathā śuklānāṃ
      kṛṣṇatvaṃ kṛṣṇānāṃ śuklatvaṃ | sthirāṇām mṛdutvaṃ | calānām acalatvam acalānāñ
      calatvaṃ | pṛthūnāṃ saṃkṣiptatvaṃ saṃkṣiptānāṃ pṛthutvaṃ | dīrghāṇāṃ hrasvatvaṃ ca
      hrasvānāṃ dīrghatā | apatanadharmmiṇāṃ patanam akasmāc
      chaityoṣṇasneharaukṣyaprastambhavaivarṇṇyāni apasarppaṇam aṅgānāṃ svebhyaḥ
      sthānebhyaḥ śarīraikadeśānām
      avasraṃsotkṣiptabhrāntapatitavimuktanirggamātigamagurulaghutvāni
      pravālavarṇṇavyaṅgaprādurbbhāvo vākasmāt sirāṇāṃ ca darśana lalāṭe nāsāvaṃśe vā
      piṭakotpattir udakotpattir nnetrarogam vināsrupravṛttir lalāṭe vā prabhātakāle
      svedapravṛttiḥ | gomayacūrṇṇaprakāśasya rajaso darśanam uttamāṅge līyanam vā
      kapotakaṅkagṛddhraprabhṛtīnāṃ mūtrapurīṣapravṛddhir abhuñjanānāṃ
      stanamūlahṛdayorassu ca śūlotpattayaḥ | madhye śūnatvam anteṣu parimlāyitvaṃ |
      viparyayo vā naṣṭahīnavikalavihṛtasvaraṃ vā vivarṇṇapuṣpaprādurbbhāvo vā
      dantanakhaśarīreṣu puṣpadarśanaṃ yasya cāpsu kaphaśakṛdretāṃsi nimajjanti yasya ca
      dṛṣṭimaṇḍale bhinnavikṛtāni rūpāṇy ālocyante snehābhyaktakeśāṅga iva yo bhāti yaś ca
      durbbalo bhaktadveṣātisārābhyām pīḍyate | kāsamānaś ca tṛṣṇātibhūtaḥ kṣīṇaś
      charddibhaktadeśayuktaḥ saphenarudhirodvāmī hatasvaraḥ śūlābhihataś ca
      manuṣyaśūnakaracaraṇo nnadveṣī srastapiṇḍakāṃsapāṇipādaḥ | yaś ca pūrvāhṇe bhuktam
      aparāhṇe ścharddayaty avidagdhaṃ sāryate vā jvarakāsābhibhūtaḥ sa śvāsān mriyate |
      vastavad vilapamāno bhūmau patati srastamuṣkaḥ stabdhaśepo bhagnagrīvaḥ
      praṇaṣṭamehaś ca manuṣyaḥ prāgviśuṣyamāṇahṛdaya ārddraśarīraḥ | yaś ca loṣṭaṃ
      loṣṭenābhihanti | kāṣṭham vā kāṣṭhena tṛṇāni vā cchinnanti | adharoṣṭham vā daśati
      uttaroṣṭham vā leḍhi | āluñcati karṇṇau keśām̐ś ca | devadvijagurusuhṛdvaidyān vā
      vidveṣṭi yasya ca vakrānuvakragā grahā garhitasthānagatāḥ | janmaṛkṣam
      vāsyolkāśanibhyām abhihanyate | rātrau vā
      gṛhadvāraśayanāsanayānavāhanamaṇiratnopakaraṇagarhitalakṣaṇanimittaprādurbbhāvo veti
      || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.32.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.32.5</label>
       bhavanti cātra ||
      <caesura/>
       cikitsyamānaḥ samyak tu vikāro yo 'bhivarddhate |
      <caesura/>
       prakṣīṇabala<pc> </pc>māṃsasya lakṣaṇan tadgatāyuṣaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.32.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.32.6</label>
       nivarttate mahāvyādhiḥ sahasā yasya dehinaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       na cāhāraphalaṃ yasya dṛśyate sa vinaśyati || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.32.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.32.7</label>
       etāni riṣṭarūpāṇi samyag budhyeta yo bhiṣak |
      <caesura/>
       sādhyāsādhyaparīkṣañ ca sa rājñaḥ sammato bhaved iti || 31 || ❈ || </l>

    </div>

    <div n="33" type="adhyāya">
     <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 33, draft based on MS H]</head>




     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.1"><label>1.33.1</label>
       athāto vāraṇīyam adhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.2"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.3</label>
       upadravais tu ye juṣṭā-vyādhayo yānty avāryatāṃ |
      <caesura/>
       rasāyanair vvinā vatsa tāṃ śṛṇv ekamanā mama || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.4</label>
       vātavyādhiḥ pramehaś ca kuṣṭhānyatha bhagandaraṃ |
      <caesura/>
       arśośmarī mūḍhagarbho bhavaty udaram aṣṭamam || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.5</label>
       aṣṭāv ete mahāntaḥ syūr vvyādhayo dustarāḥ sadā | prāṇamāṃsakṣayaḥ śophas tṛṣṇā
      ccharddir jvaras tathā || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.6</label>
       atīsāraś ca mūrcchā ca hikkāśvāsas tathaiva ca |
      <caesura/>
       etair upadravair jjuṣṭān sarvvān etān vivarjayet || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.7</label>
       śūnaṃ suptatvacam bhagnaṅ kampādhmānanipīḍitaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       rujārttam antañ ca naram vātavyādhir vvināśayet || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.8</label>
       yathoktopadravāviṣṭam atiprasrutam eva ca |
      <caesura/>
       piṭakāpīḍitaṃ gāḍhaṃ prameho hanti mānavaṃ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.9</label>
       prabhinnaṃ prasrutāṅgañ ca raktanetraṃ hatasvaraṃ |
      <caesura/>
       pañcakarmmaguṇātītaṃ kuṣṭhaṃ hanti hi kuṣṭhinaṃ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.11</label>
       vātamūtrapurīṣāṇi krimayaḥ śukram eva ca |
      <caesura/>
       bhagandarāt prasravanti sa naśyati bhagandarī || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.10</label>
       tṛṣṇarocakaśūlārttam atiprasrutaśoṇitaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       śophātīsārasaṃyuktaṃ durnāmā kṣapayen naraṃ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.12</label>
       praśūnanābhivṛṣaṇaṃ vaddhamūtrarujāturaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       aśmarī kṣapayaty āśu sikatāśarkkarānvitaṃ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.14</label>
       pārśvabhaṅgānnavidveṣaḥ śophātīsārapīḍitam |
      <caesura/>
       vivarjayed udariṇam virikto yo 'bhipūryate || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.13</label>
       yonīsamvaraṇaṃ saṅgaḥ kukṣo makkallasaṃjñitaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       hanyuḥ striyaṃ mūḍhaga-rvbhe yathoktāś cāpy upadravāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.15</label>
       visaṃjñas tām yate yas tu śete nipati-to yathā |
      <caesura/>
       śītārddito 'ntaruṣṇaś ca jvareṇa mriyate naraḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.16"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.16</label>
       yo hṛṣṭaromā raktākṣo hṛdi saṃghātaśūlavān |
      <caesura/>
       vaktreṇa cocchvasiti taṃ jvaro hanti mānavaṃ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.17</label>
       hikkāśvāsa samāyuktaṃ mūḍham vibhrāntalocanaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       santatocchvāsinaṃ kṣīṇaṃ naraṃ kṣapayate jvaraḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.18"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.19</label>
       śvāsaśūlapipāsārtaṃ-kṣīṇañ jvaranipīḍitaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       viśeṣeṇa naraṃ vṛddham atīsāro vināśayet || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.20</label>
       śuklākṣamannadveṣṭāram ūrddhaśvāsanipīḍitam |
      <caesura/>
       kṛcchreṇa bahu mehantaṃ yakṣmā hantīha mānavaṃ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.21</label>
       śvāsaśūlapipāsānnavidveṣo granthimūḍhatā |
      <caesura/>
       jāyate durvvalatvaṃ ca gulmino maraṇāya vai|| </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.22"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.22</label>
       ādhmānaṃ vaddhaniṣyandaṃ ccharddihikkātṛṣānvitam |
      <caesura/>
       rujāśvāsasamāyuktaṃ vidradhir nnāśayet naraṃ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.23"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.23</label>
       pāṇḍudantanakho yastu pāṇḍunetraś ca mānavaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       pāṇḍusaṃghātadarśī ca pāṇḍurogī vinaśyati || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.24"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.24</label>
       lohitañ charddayed yas tu bahuśo lohitekṣaṇaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       lohito 'ṅgāradarśī ca mriyate raktapaittikaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.25"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.25</label>
       avāco pi savāco 'pi kṣīṇamānsavalo naraḥ |
      <caesura/>
       jāgarūko kṣyāsandeham unmādena vinaśyati || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.33.26"><label>1931 ed. 1.33.26</label>
       apasmarantam bahuśaḥ prakṣīṇañ calitaṃ bhruvaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       netrābhyāñ ca vikurvvāṇa-m apasmāro vināśayet ||</l>
     <p ana="trailer"> 33 ||</p>
    </div>

    <div n="34" type="adhyāya">
     <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 34, draft based on MS H]</head>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.1"><label>1.34.1</label>
       athāto yuktasenīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.1.1"><label>1.34.1.1</label>
       dhanvantarim mahāprājñaṃ sarvvaśāstraviśāradaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       caraṇāv upasaṃgṛhya suśrutaḥ paripṛcchati ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.2"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.3</label>
       yuktasenasya nṛpateḥ parānabhijighāṃsataḥ |
      <caesura/>
       bhiṣajā rakṣaṇaṃ kāryaṃ yathā tad brūhi me mune ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.3.1"><label>1.34.3.1</label>
       tasya tad vacanaṃ śrutvā prābravīd bhiṣajām varaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.4</label>
       vijigīṣuḥ sahāmātyair yātrāyuktaḥ prayatnataḥ |
      <caesura/>
       rakṣitavyo viśeṣeṇa viṣādeva narādhipaḥ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.5</label>
       panthānam udakañ chāyāṃ bhaktaṃ yavasamindhanaṃ ||
      <caesura/>
       duṣayanty arayas tāni jānīyāc chodhanīya ca |
      <caesura/>
       tasya liṅgaṃ cikitsāñ ca kalpasthāne pravakṣyate ||</l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.6</label>
       ekottaraṃ mṛtyuśatam atharvvāṇaḥ pracakṣate |
      <caesura/>
       tatraikaḥ kālasaṃyuktaḥ śeṣās tv āgantavaḥ smṛtāḥ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.7</label>
       doṣāgantunimittebhyo rasamantraviśāradau |
      <caesura/>
       rakṣatāṃ nṛpatin nityaṃ yatnād vaidyapurohitau ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.8</label>
       brahmāvedāṅgamaṣṭāṅgam āyurvvedam pracakṣate |
      <caesura/>
       tasmāt purohitamate vartteta bhiṣag ātmavān ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.9</label>
       saṅkaraḥ sarvvavarṇṇānāṃ vināśo dharmmakarmmiṇāṃ |
      <caesura/>
       prajanām api kṛcchrāṇi bhavanti nṛpanāśataḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.10</label>
       puruṣāṇān nṛpānāñ ca kevalan tulyamūrttitā |
      <caesura/>
       ājñātyāgaḥ kṣamā dhairyam vikramaś cāpy amānuṣaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.11</label>
       tasmād devam ivābhīkṣṇam vāṅmanaḥ karmabhiḥ śubhaiḥ |
      <caesura/>
       cintayet nṛpatim vaidyaḥ śreyāṃsīcchan vicakṣaṇaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.12</label>
       skandhāvāre ca mahati rājaveśma samīpataḥ |
      <caesura/>
       bhavet sannihito vaidyaḥ sarvvopakaraṇānvitaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.13</label>
       tatrastham enan dhvajavad yaśaḥkhyātibhir ucchritaṃ ||
      <caesura/>
       upasarppantyamohena viṣaśalyāmayārdditāḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.14</label>
       svatantrakuśalo 'nyeṣu śāstrārtheṣv abahiḥ kṛtaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       vaidyo dhvajam ivābhāti nṛpatadvidyapūjitaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.15</label>
       vaidyo vyādhyupasṛṣṭaś ca bhaiṣajam paricārakaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       ete pādāś cikitsāyāḥ karmmasādhanahetavaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.16"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.16</label>
       guṇavadbhis tribhiḥ pādaiś caturthyo guṇavān bhiṣak |
      <caesura/>
       vyādhim alpena kālena mahāntam api sādhayet ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.17</label>
       vaidyahīnās trayaḥ pādā guṇavanto 'pyapārthakāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       udgātṛhotṛbrahmāṇo yathādhvaryam vinādhvare ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.18</label>
       vaidyas tu guṇavāneko yāpayed āturaṃ sadā |
      <caesura/>
       plavam paricaran dhīraḥ karṇṇadhāram ivāmbhasi ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.19</label>
       tatvopagataśāstrārtho dṛṣṭakarmmā svayaṅkṛtī |
      <caesura/>
       laghuhastaḥ śuciḥ sūraḥ sajjopaskarabheṣajaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.20</label>
       pratyutpannamatir ddhīmān vyavasāyī viśāradaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       satyadharmmaparo yaś ca sabhiṣak pāda ucyate ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.21</label>
       āyuṣmān satvavān sādhyo dravyavān mitravān api |
      <caesura/>
       vaidyavākyakṛd āstiṣko vyādhitaḥ pāda ucyate ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.22"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.22</label>
       praśastadeśasaṃbhūtaṃ praśaste kāla uddhṛtaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       yuktamātram manaskāntaṅ gandhavarṇṇarasānvitaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.23"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.23</label>
       doṣaghnamaglāninikaram avikārya viparyayaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       samīkṣya dattaṅ kāle ca bheṣajam pāda ucyate ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.34.24"><label>1931 ed. 1.34.24</label>
       snigdho 'jugupsur bbalavānyukto vyādhitarakṣaṇe |
      <caesura/>
       vaidyavākyakṛdaśrāntaḥ pādaḥ paricaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||</l>

     <p ana="trailer">layka ||</p>
    </div>

    <div n="35" type="adhyāya">
     <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 35, draft based on MS H]</head>



     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.1</label>
       athāta āturopakramaṇīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.2"/>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.3</label>
       āturam upakramamāṇena vaidyenāyurādāv eva tāvat parīsatyāyuṣi
      vyādhyṛtvagnivayodehasatvavalasātmyaprakṛtibheṣajadeśān parīkṣeta | </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.4</label>
       tatra
      mahāpāṇipādapṛṣṭhastanāgrasukhadarśanaskandhalalāṭadīrghāṅguliparvvocchvāsaprekṣaṇavāhum
      vistīrṇṇabhrūs tanāntaroraskaṃ hṛsvajaṅghāmeḍhragrīvaṅ
      gambhīrasatvasvaranāsimanuccair vaddhas tanm upacitamahāromaṃ romasakarṇṇe pārśva
      mastakaṃ snātānuliptaṃ mūrddham ānūpūrvyo paścāc ca viśuṣyamāṇahṛdayam puruṣañ
      jānīyād dīrghāyuḥ khalv ayam iti | tam ekāntena upakramet | tatra tail laikṣaṇair
      viparītair alpayum miśrair mmadhyam āyur iti || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.5</label>
       bhavanti cātra ||
      <caesura/>
       gūḍhasandhisirāsnāyuḥ saṃhatāṅgaḥ sthirendriyaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       uttarottarasukṣetro yaḥ sa dīrghāyur ucyate || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.6</label>
       garbhāt prabhṛtyarogo yaḥ śanaiḥ samabhivarddhate |
      <caesura/>
       śarīrajñānavijñānaiḥ sa dīrghāyuḥ samāsataḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.7</label>
       madhyamasyāyuṣo jñāna mata ūrdhvan nibodha me |
      <caesura/>
       adhastād akṣayor yasya rekhāḥ suvyaktam āyatāḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.8</label>
       dve vā tisro 'dhikā vāpi pādau karṇau ca māṃsalau |
      <caesura/>
       nāsāgram ūrdhvañ ca bhavet rekhāś ca pṛṣṭhataḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.9</label>
       yasya syus tasya vijñeyam āyur bhavati saptatiḥ |
      <caesura/>
       jaghanyaś cāyuṣo jñāna mata ūrdhvan nibodha me || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.10</label>
       hṛsvāni yasya parvvāṇi sumahac cāpi mehanaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       avalīḍham uroyaś ca na ca syāt pṛṣṭham āyataṃ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.11</label>
       ūrdhvañ ca śravaṇau sthānān nāsā coccā śarīriṇaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       hasato jalpato vāpi dantamānsam pradṛśyate || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.12ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.12ab</label>
       atha punar āyuṣo vijñānārtham aṅgapratyaṅgapramāṇasāra anupadekṣyāmaḥ || tatra
      aṅgātyantarādhiśakthivāhuśirāṃsi tad avayavāḥ pratyaṅgāni svair aṅgulaiḥ
      pādāṅguṣṭhapradeśinyau dvaṅgulāyate | pradeśinyās tu madhyamānāmikākaniṣṭhikā
      pūrvvataḥ | pañcañ bhāgahīnācaturaṅgulāyate | pañcaṅgulavismṛte | </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.12cd"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.13"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.14"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.15"/>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.16cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.16cd</label>
       snigdhatāmranakhanayanajihoṣṭhapāṇipādatalaṃ | raktnena suprasanna mṛdutvagromāṇaṃ
      tvaṣāṃ pūrvva prādhānyād āyuḥ saubhāgyāpayogāyeti ||</l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.16.1"><label>1.35.16.1</label>
       sāmānyato 'ṅgapratyaṅgapramāṇād atha sārataḥ |
      <caesura/>
       parīkṣyāyuḥ sunipuṇo bhiṣak sidhyati karmmasu || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.18</label>
       vyādhiviśeṣās tu prāg abhihitāḥ sarvvaṃ evaite trividhā bhavanti | sādhyā yāpyāḥ
      pratyākhyeyāś ceti | tatra sādhya yāpya pratyākhye yān vyādhīn bhūyatri vidhā
      parīkṣeta | kimayam aupasargikaḥ prāk kevalo 'nyalakṣaṇa iti | taraupasargiko nāma
      yaḥ pūrvvotpannaṃ vyādhiñ jaghanyakālajāto vyādhir upasṛjati | sa tat mūle sa
      evopadravasaṃjñaḥ | prāk kevalo nāma | yaḥ prāgevotpanno vyādhirar
      apūrvarūpopadravaś ca | anya lakṣaṇo nāma yo bhaviṣyat khyāpakaḥ sa
      pūrvvarūpasaṃjñaḥ | tatra sopadravam anyonyāvirodhenopacaret | valavantaram
      upadravam vā prāk kevalaṃ yathāsvam pratikurvīta | anye lakṣaṇe tv ādivyādhau yathā
      yathāvat prayateta | </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.19</label>
       bhavati cātra |
      <caesura/>
       nāsti rogo vinā doṣaṃ yasmāt tasmāc cikitsakaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       anuktam api doṣāṇāṃ liṅgair doṣam upācaret || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.20</label>
       prāg abhihitā ṛtavaḥ | </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.21</label>
       śīta śītapratīkāram uṣṇe coṣṇanivāraṇaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       kālaprāptāṅ kriyāṃ kuryāt kriyākālan na hāpayet || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.22"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.22</label>
       apāpte vā kriyākāle prāpte vā na kṛtā kriyā |
      <caesura/>
       hīnātiriktā ca kṛtā sādyeṣv api na sidhyati || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.23"/>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.24"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.24</label>
       prāg abhihito 'gnir annābhipācakaḥ sa pañcavidho bhavati || samo doṣābhipanno
      vikriyām āpanna iti || viṣamo vātena | tīkṣṇa pittena | mandaḥ śleṣmaṇā | samaḥ
      sarvvaiḥ samar iti || tatra yo yathā kālam annam upayuktaṃ samya pacati sa samaḥ |
      yas tu kadācit samyak pacati kadācid asamyak pacaty ādhmānaśūlātīsārapravāhaṇāni
      kṛtvā pacati sa viṣamaḥ | yas tu prabhūtam apy annam upayuktam āśu pacati sa tīkṣṇaḥ
      | sarvābhivardhamāno 'tyagnir bhavati || muhumr mmuhuḥ prabhūtataram annam upayuktam
      āśutaraṃ pacati pākānte ca galatālvoṣṭhapraśoṣadāhasantāpān janayati asyaiva
      bhasmaka iti vyapadiśanti || yas tv alpam apy annam upayuktam
      udaraśirogauravakāsaśvāsacchardiprasekagātrasadanāni kṛtvā mahā kālena pacati sa
      mandaḥ || bha || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.25"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.25</label>
       viṣamo vātajān rogāñ stīkṣṇaḥ pittanimittajān |
      <caesura/>
       karoty agnis tathā mando vikārān kaphasambhavān || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.26"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.26</label>
       tatra same rakṣaṇaṃ kurvvīta || viṣamaṃ lavaṇāmlaiḥ snehayuktaiḥ kriyāviśeṣair
      upacaret || tīkṣṇam madhurasnigdhayuktair vvirecanaiś ca | evam evāty agnim viśeṣeṇa
      māhiyaird dadhikṣīrasarppibhir iti || mande kaṭutiktakaṣāyair vvamanaiś ca || bha || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.27"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.27</label>
       audāryo bhagavān agniḥ pāvako 'nnasya ceśvaraḥ |
      <caesura/>
       saukṣmyādrasānādadāno vivektun neha śakyate || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.28"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.28</label>
       prāṇāpānasamānais tu sarvvataḥ pavanais tribhiḥ |
      <caesura/>
       dhyāmate pālyate cāpi svāṃ svāṃ gatim avasthitaiḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.29"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.29</label>
       vayas tu trividham vālyaṃ madhyam vṛddham iti | tatronaṣoḍaśavarṣād vālābhavanti |
      te trividhāḥ kṣīrapāḥ kṣīrānnādā annādā iti | ṣoḍaśasaptatyor antare madhyasvayas
      tasyad vikalpo vṛddhir yauvanaṃ sampūrṇṇateti | tatrāviṃśater vṛddhir ātriṃśato
      yauvanam ācatvāriṃśataḥ sarvvadhātvindriyasampūrṇṇetiti || ata ūrdhvaṃ hā nir
      bhavati yāvadā saptateḥ | saptatyāsrūrdhaṃ kṣīyamāṇadhātvindriyavalavīryotsāho
      'nyahani valīpalitakhālity akāsaśvāsaprabhṛtibhir upadravair abhibhūyamānaṃ
      sarvvakriyāsvasamarthā jīrṇṇāgāram ivāvasīdati | tam vṛddham ācakṣate | </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.30"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.30</label>
       uttarottarāsu ca vayo 'vastjāsu uttarottare bheṣajamātraprayogaḥ | ṛte parihānim
      kurvanti ||</l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.31"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.31</label>
       bhavanti cātra |
      <caesura/>
       vāle vivarddhate ślemā madhyame pittam eva tu |
      <caesura/>
       bhūyiṣṭham vardhate vāyurvvṛddhe tad vīkṣya yojayet || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.32"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.32</label>
       agnikṣāravirekais tu vālavṛddhau vivarjjayet |
      <caesura/>
       tatsādhyeṣu vikāreṣu mṛdvīṃ kuryāt kriyāṃ śanaiḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.33"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.33</label>
       dehaḥ sthūlaḥ kṛśo madhya iti prāgabhitaṃ || ca || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.34"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.34</label>
       karṣayed vṛhayed c cāpi sadā sthūlakṛśau narau |
      <caesura/>
       madhyasya rakṣaṇañ cāpi kurvvīta satatam bhiṣak || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.35"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.35</label>
       valan tvanabhihataguṇaṃ daurvvalyan tu svabhāvadoṣajarābhir āpekṣikam bhavati ||
      yasmād valavataḥ sarvvakriyāpratipattis tasmād valapradhānam adhikaraṇānāṃ | </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.36"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.36</label>
       kecit kṛśāḥ prāṇavantaḥ sthūlāś cālpavalā narāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       tasmāt sthiratvavyāyāmer vvalam vaidyaḥ pratarkkayet || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.37"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.37</label>
       satvan tu vyasanabhayābhyudayakriyādisthāneṣv avikam vakaram bhavati || ca || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.38"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.38</label>
       satvavān sahate sarvvaṃ saṃstabhyamānaḥ parair n naraḥ |
      <caesura/>
       rājasaṃstabhyambhyamāno 'pi sahate naiva tāmasaḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.39"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.39</label>
       prakṛtim bheṣajañ cānyatro pademaḥ | sātmyāni tu deśajāni rogar tu
      vyāyāmodakarasadivāspnaprabhṛtīni prakṛtiviruddhānyapi yānyanāvādhakarāṇi bhavanti
      || bha || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.40"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.40</label>
       yo rasaḥ kalpito yasya sukhatāṃ yāti sevitaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       vyāyāmajātam anyad vā tat sātmyam iti nirddiśet || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.41"/>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.42"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.42</label>
       deśas tv ānūpo jāṅgalaḥ sādhāraṇa iti trividhā bhavati | tatra
      nimnonnatavahūdakanadīvarṣagahanamṛdūśītalo vahūmahāparvatavṛkṣo
      mṛdusukumāropacitaśarīramanuṣyaprāyo vātakapharogabhūyiṣṭhaś cānūpaḥ ||
       vakt<pc> </pc>ākāsam avitaralālpa<pc
      > </pc>kaṇṭakavṛkṣavarṣaprasravaṇodapānaprāyoṣṇadārūṇavātapraviralālpaśailasthirakṛśaśarīramanuṣyaprāyo
      vātapittaro gabhūyiṣṭhaś ca jāṅgalaḥ | ubhayalakṣaṇas sādhāraṇasya pradhāna iti || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.43"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.43</label>
       bhavati cātra ||
      <caesura/>
       samāḥ sādhāraṇe yasmād varṣaśītoṣṇamārūtāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       doṣāṇāṃ samatā vāpi tasmāt sādhāraṇo varaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.45"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.45</label>
       ucite varttamānasya nāsti deśakṛtam bhayaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       āhārasvapnaceṣṭādau tad deśaḥ saguṇa satīti || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.46"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.46</label>
       deśaprakṛti sātmyartva viparītācirotthitaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       sampattau bheṣajādīnām valasatvāyuṣān tathā || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.47"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.47</label>
       kevalaḥ samadehāgneḥ sukhasādhyatamo mataḥ |
      <caesura/>
       ato 'nyathāpy asādhyaḥ syāt kṛcchro vyāmiśralakṣaṇaḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.48"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.48</label>
       kriyāyās tu guṇālābhe kriyām anyāṃ prayojayet |
      <caesura/>
       pūrvvasyāṃ śāntavegāyān na kriyāsaṃaro hitaḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.44"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.44</label>
       na tathā balavantaḥ syuḥ jalajā vā sthalāhṛtāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       svadeśe nicitā doṣās tv anyasmin kopam āgatāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.50"><label>1931 ed. 1.35.50</label>
       ucite varttamānasya nāsti deśakṛtam bhayaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       āhārasvapnaceṣṭādau taddeśaḥ saguṇa satīti || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.35.trailer" ana="letter-numerals">ity adhyāya 35</l>

    <div n="37" type="adhyāya" corresp="1.36 in NAK 5-333">

     <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 37 (<foreign xml:lang="sa"
      >miśrakannāmādhyāyaṃ</foreign>) which is located between adhyāyas 35 and 36 in the
      Nepalese version, but is still numbered 37. Draft based on MS H]</head>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.1</label>
       athāto miśrakannāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.2"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.3</label>
       mātuluṅgāgnimanthau ca bhadradāru mahauṣadhaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       ahiṃsā caiva rāsnā ca pralepo vātaśophahā || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.4</label>
       dūrvvā ca nalamūlañ ca madhukañ candanan tathā |
      <caesura/>
       śītalāś ca gaṇāḥ sarvve pralepaḥ pittaśophahā || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.5</label>
       āgantuje raktaje ca lepa eṣo 'bhipūjitaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       vidhirvviṣaghno viṣaje pittaghno 'bhihitas tathā || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.6</label>
       ajagandhāśvagandhā ca kālā śarala eva ca |
      <caesura/>
       eke ṣikājaśṛṅgī ca pralepaḥ śleṣmaśophahā || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.7</label>
       ete ca varggā lodhrañ ca pathyā piṇḍīkṛtāstuyaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       anantā ceti lepo 'yaṃ śophesarvvakṛtehitaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.8</label>
       snigdho 'mlalavaṇo vāte koṣṇaḥ śītaḥ payoyutaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       pitte 'thoṣṇeh kaphe kṣāramūtrāḍhyastatpraśāntaye || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.9</label>
       śaṇaśigruphalātasī tilakalkāś ca sarṣaṣāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       śaktavaḥ kiṇvamuṣṇāni dravyāṇyapi ca pācanam || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.10</label>
       ciribilvāgniko dantī citrako hayamārakaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       kapotakaṅkagṛddhrāṇām purīṣāṇi vidāraṇe || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.10ef"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.10ef</label>
       kṣāradravyāṇi vā yāni kṣāro vā dāraṇaṃ paraṃ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.11</label>
       dravyāṇām picchilānāṃ tu tvahyūlāni prapīḍanaṃ ||
      <caesura/>
       yavagodhūmamāṣāṇāṃ cūrṇṇāni ca samāsataḥ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.12</label>
       śaṅkhinyaṃ koṭhasumanāḥkaravīraṃsuvarccalā ||
      <caesura/>
       śodhanāni kaṣāyāṇi varggaś cāragvadhādikaḥ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.13</label>
       ajagandhājaśṛṅgī ca gavākṣī lāṅgalāhvayā ||
      <caesura/>
       pūtīkaś citrakaḥ pāṭhā viḍaṅgailāhareṇavaḥ | </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.14</label>
       kaṭutrikaṃ yavakṣāro lavaṇāni manaḥśilā ||
      <caesura/>
       kāśīsan tṛvṛtā dantī haritālaṃ surāṣṭrikā | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.15</label>
       saṃśodhanīnāṃ varttīnāṃ dravyāṇy etāni nirddiśet ||
      <caesura/>
       dravyeṣveteṣu kurvvīta kalkān api ca śodhanān | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.16ab"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.17</label>
       arkottamāsudhākṣīraṃ piṣṭvā kṣārottamām api ||
      <caesura/>
       jātīmūlaṃ haridre dve kāsīsaṃ kaṭurohiṇī | </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.16cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.16cd</label>
       pūrvvoddiṣṭeṣu cāṅgeṣu kuryāt saṃśodhanaṃ ghṛtaṃ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.18ab"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.18cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.18cd</label>
       mayūrako rājavṛkṣo nimbaḥ kośātakī tilā | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.19</label>
       bṛhatī kaṇṭakārī ca haritālam manaḥśilā ||
      <caesura/>
       śodhanāni ca yāni syus taile yojyāni śodhane | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.20</label>
       kāsīse saindhave kiṇve vacāyāṃ rajanīdvaye ||
      <caesura/>
       śodhanāṅgeṣu cānyeṣu cūrṇṇaṃ kurvvīta śodhanaṃ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.21</label>
       sālasārādisāreṣu paṭolatriphalāsu ca ||
      <caesura/>
       rasakriyā vidhātavyā śodhanī śodhaneṣu ca | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.22"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.22</label>
       śrīveṣṭake sarjjarase sarale devadāruṇi ||
      <caesura/>
       sāreṣv api ca kurvvīta matimān vraṇadhūpanaṃ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.23"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.23</label>
       kaṣāyāṇāmanuṣṇānān drvyāṇān tvakṣu sādhitaṃ ||
      <caesura/>
       śṛtaśīta kaṣāyam vā ropanārthe praśasyate | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.24"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.24</label>
       somāmṛtāśvagandhāsu kākolyādau gaṇe tathā ||
      <caesura/>
       kṣīrīpraroheṣv api ca varttayo ropaṇā hitāḥ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.25"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.25</label>
       samaṅgā somasaralā somavalkāḥ sacandanāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       kākolyādiś ca kalkāḥ syuḥ praśastā vraṇaropaṇe | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.26"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.26</label>
       pṛthakparṇṇyātmaguptā ca haridre mālatī sitā ||
      <caesura/>
       kākolyādiś ca yojyāḥ syuḥ praśastā ropaṇe ghṛte | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.27"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.27</label>
       kālānusāryaguruṇī haridrā bhadradāru ca ||
      <caesura/>
       priyaṅgavaś ca lodhrañ ca taile yojyāni ropaṇe | </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.28"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.28</label>
       kaṅguka triphalā lodhraṃ kāśīsaṃ śravaṇāhvayā ||
      <caesura/>
       dhavośvakarṇṇayos tvak ca ropaṇe cūrṇṇamiṣyate | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.29"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.30" met="hyper metrical"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.30 hyper
       metrical</label>
       tvakṣu nyagrodhavarggasya triphalās tathaiva ca ||
      <caesura/>
       rasakriyāṃ ropaṇārthe vidadhīta yathākramaṃ |<anchor n="SS.1.37.30-n1"/>
     </l>


     <ab corresp="#SS.1.37.30" type="apparatus">
      <list type="notes">
       <item corresp="#SS.1.37.30-n1">Hypermetrical.</item>
      </list>
     </ab>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.31"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.31</label>
       apāmārggo 'svagandhā ca tālapattrī suvarccalā ||
      <caesura/>
       utsādane praśasyante kākolyādiś ca yo gaṇaḥ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.32"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.32</label>
       kāsīsaṃ saindhavan kutthaṃ kuruvindam manaḥśilā ||
      <caesura/>
       kukkuṭāṇḍakapālāni sumanomukulāni ca | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.33ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.33ab</label>
       phale śairīṣakārañjair ddhātucūrṇāni yāni ca || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.33.1"><label>1.37.33.1</label>
       suvarccikātha kāśīsaṃ saindhavaṃ kṣāram eva ca | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.33cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.33cd</label>
       vraṇeṣūtsannamāṃseṣu praśastāny avasādane || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.33.2"><label>1.37.33.2</label>
       ālepana nicūrṇṇāni pradadyāt sakalāni vai | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.34"><label>1931 ed. 1.37.34</label>
       samastaṃ varggamarddham vā yathālābham athāpi vā ||
      <caesura/>
       prayuñjīta bhiṣak prājño yathoddiṣṭeṣu karmmasu || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.37.trailer">37</l>


    </div>


    <div n="36" type="adhyāya" corresp="1.37 in NAK 5-333">

     <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 37 (bhūmipravibhāgavijñānīyam) of the Nepalese version,
      adhyāya 36 in the vulgate. Draft based on MS H]</head>

     <note>There are large differences between the Ācārya 1931 and 1938 editions version
      of Cakrapāṇidatta's commentary on this adhyāya.</note>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.36.1</label>
       athāto bhūmipravibhāgavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.2"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.36.3</label>
       svabhraśarkkarāśmaviṣamavalmīkaśmaśānāghatadevatāyatanasikatoṣairar
      anupahatāmanūṣarāmabhaṃgurāmadūrodakāṃ snigdhāṃ prarohavatīṃ mṛdvīṃ sthirāṃ samāṃ
      gaurīṃ lohitāṃ vā bhūmim auṣadha grahaṇāya parīkṣeta || tasyāṅ jātam api hi
      krimaviṣaśastrātapapavanadahanatoyasambādhamārggair anupahatamekasāraṃ puṣṭam
      avagāḍhamūlaṃ cauṣadhamādadyād ity eṣāṃ bhūmiparīkṣāvibhāgaḥ sāmānyaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.36.4</label>
       viśeṣatas tu tatra aśmavatī sthirā gurvvī śdhāmā kṛṣṇā vā sthūlatṛṇaśasyaprāyāḥ
      svaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā | snigdhā śītalāsannodakā snigdhatṛṇaśasyākomalavṛkṣaprāyā
      śuklāmbuguṇabhūyiṣṭhā || nānāvarṇṇā laghvāśmavatī
      viralālyapāṇḍuraprarohāgniguṇabhūyiṣṭhā || rūkṣā bhasmarāsabhavarṇṇā
      kṣatanuvṛkṣakoṭarālparasaprāyānilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā || mṛdvī
      samāvyabhravatyavyaktarasajalā mahāparvvatavṛkṣaprāryā syāmā cākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhā || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.36.5</label>
       tatra kecid ācāryāḥ prāvṛṭvarṣāśaraddhemantavasantagrīṣmeṣu yathāsaṃkhyam
      mūlapattratvacakṣīrasāraphalāny ādadīta || tat tu na samyak kasmāt saumyāgneyatvāj
      jagataḥ | saumyāny auṣadhāni saumyeṣv ṛtuṣv ādadīta | āgneyāny āgneyeṣv evam
      avyāpannāni bhavanti || saumyāny auṣadhāni saumyeṣv ṛtuṣu gṛhītāni
      somaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau madhuratarāsnigdhatarāṇiśītatarāṇi bhavanti | āgneyāny
      auṣadhāni āgneyeṣv ṛtuṣu gṛhītānyagniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau uṣṇatarāṇi kaṭutarāṇi
      rūkṣatarāṇi bhavanti | </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.36.6</label>
       tatrā pṛthivῑguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ bhūmau jātāni virecanadravyāṇyādadīta |
      agnyanilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāñ ca vamanadravyāṇi | ubhayaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām
      ubhayatobhāgaharāṇi | ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ saṃśamanāny evam balavattarāṇi bhavanti
      | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.36.7</label>
       sarvvāṇi cābhinavānyatra madhughṛtapippalīviḍaṅgebhya iti || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.9" corresp="1.36.11 of 1938 ed"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.10" corresp="1.36.12 of 1938 ed"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.11" corresp="1.36.13 of 1938 ed"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.12" corresp="1.36.14 of 1938 ed"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.13" corresp="1.36.15 of 1938 ed"/>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.14" corresp="1.36.8 of 1938 ed"><label>1931 ed. 1.36.14"
       corresp="1.36.8 of 1938 ed</label>
       viḍaṅga pippalī kṣaudraṃ sarpiś cāpyanavaṃ hitaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       śeṣam anyat tv abhinavaṃ gṛhṇīyād doṣavarjjitaṃ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.15" corresp="1.36.16 of 1938 ed"><label>1931 ed. 1.36.15"
       corresp="1.36.16 of 1938 ed</label>
       jaṅgamānāṃ vayaḥsthānāñ carmaromanakhādikaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       kṣīramūtrapurīṣāṇi jīrṇṇāhāreṣu saṃharet || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.16" corresp="1.36.17 of 1938 ed"><label>1931 ed. 1.36.16"
       corresp="1.36.17 of 1938 ed</label>
       plotamṛdbhāṇḍaphalakaṃ saṅkuvinyastabheṣajān |
      <caesura/>
       praśastāyān diśi śucau bheṣajāgāram iṣyate || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.36.8" corresp="1.36.10 of 1938 ed"><label>1931 ed. 1.36.8"
       corresp="1.36.10 of 1938 ed</label>
       gopālās tāpasā vyādhā ye cānye vanacāriṇaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       mūlāhārāś ca ye teṣāṃ bheṣajavyaktir iṣyate iti || </l>
    </div>

    <div n="38" type="adhyāya">
     <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 38, draft based on MS H]</head>





     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.1</label>
       athāto dravyasaṅgrahaṇīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.2"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.3</label>
       pañcatriṃśad dravyagaṇā bhavanti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.4</label>
       tad yathā | vidārigandhā vidārīviśvadevā sahadevāśvadaṃṣṭrā pṛthakparṇṇī śatāvarīe
      śārivā jīvakarṣabho kṣudrasahā bṛhatyau punarnnaiveraṇḍahaṃsapādīvṛścikālyṛṣabhī
      śṛgālavinnā ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.5</label>
       vidārigandhādirayaṅ gaṇaḥ pittānilāpahaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       śophagulmāṅgamarddorddhvaśvāsakāsavināśanaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.6</label>
       āragvadhamadanaphalagopaghoṇṭākaṇṭakī
      kaṇṭakārīkuṭajaphalapāṭhāpāṭalīmūrvvāsaptaparṇṇanimbakuraṇaaṭakaguḍūcīcitrakaśārṅgaṣṭādvikarañjapaṭolakirātatiktakāḥ
      suṣavī ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.7</label>
       āragvadhādirity eṣa gaṇaḥ śleṣmaviṣāpahaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       mehakuṣṭajvaravamīkaṇḍūghno vraṇaśodhanaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.8"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.9"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.10"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.11"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.12">śālasārājakarṇṇakhadirakramubhūrjjameṣaśṛṅgīti
      nisacandanakucandanaśiṃśapā śirīṣāsanadhavārjjunanaktamālapūtīkāś ca karṇṇagurūṇi
      kālīyakañ ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.13</label>
       śālasārādir ity eṣa gaṇaḥ kuṣṭhavināśanaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       mehapāṇḍvāmayaharaḥ kaphamedoviśoṣaṇaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.13.1">
      varuṇārttagalamadhuśigrutarkkārīmeṣaśṛṅgīpūtīkanaktamālapāṭalāgnimanthaśairīyakadvayaṃ
      bimbīcitraśatāvarībilvājaśṛṅgīdarbbhābṛhatīdvayañ ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.13.2"><label>1.38.13.2</label>
       varuṇādigaṇopyeṣa kaphamedo viśoṣaṇaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       vinihanti śiraḥ śūlaṃ gulmābhyantaravidradhīḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.13.3"><label>1.38.13.3</label>
       vīratarasahacaradvayasairīyakadarbbhavṛkṣādanīgundrānalakuśakāśāśmabhedakāgni
      manthamoraṭavasukavisarabhallūkakurūṭikendīvarakapotavaṅkāśvadaṃṣṭrā ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.13.4"><label>1.38.13.4</label>
       vīratarādirity eṣa gaṇo vātavikārahṛt |
      <caesura/>
       śarkkarāśmarihāmūtrakṛcchrāghātarujāpahaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.14</label>
       lodhraśāvaralodhrapalāśakuṭannaṭāśokakaṭphalailavāluśallakījiṅjiṇīka dambākadalī
      ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.15</label>
       eṣa lodhrādiko nāmnā medaḥ kaphaharogaṇaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       yonidoṣaharastambhī vaṇyo viṣavināśanaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.16"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.16</label>
       arkkālarkkakarañjadvayanāgadantīmayūrakabhārggīrāsnendrapuṣpīkṣudrasvetābhallūkamahāsvetāvṛścikālyā
      lavaṇātāpasavṛkṣaś ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.17</label>
       arkkādis tu gaṇo hyeṣa kaphamedoviṣāpahaḥ ||
      <caesura/>
       krimikuṣṭhapraśamano viśeṣād vraṇaśodhanaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.19</label>
       surasāsvetasurasāphaṇijhjakārjjakabhūstṛṇasugandhakakālamālakuṭherakakṣavakakharapusaviḍaṅga
      ṅgapāṭhaletikaṭphalasurasīnirgguṇḍīphuluphalondurukarṇṇī phañjīprajībalākākamācyo
      viṣamuṣṭiś ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.19</label>
       surasādirgaṇo hyeṣa kaphahṛt krimisūdanaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       pratisyāyāruciḥ kāsaśvāsaghno vraṇaśodhanaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.20</label>
       muṣkakapalāśadhavacitrakamadanavṛkṣaśiṃśapāvajravṛkṣastriphalā ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.21</label>
       muṣkakādir ggaṇo hyeṣa medoghnaḥ śukradoṣahā |
      <caesura/>
       mehārśaḥ pāṇḍurogaghnaḥ śarkrāśmarināśanaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.22"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.22</label>
       pippalīpippalīmūlaṃcavyacitrakaśṛṅgaveramaricahareṇukailājamodendrayavapāṭhājīrakasarṣapa
      mahānimbahiṃgubhārggāmadhurasātiviṣāviḍaṅgakaṭurohiṇī ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.23"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.23</label>
       pippalyādiḥ kaphaharaḥ pratisyāya marīcakaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       anilañ cāpi gulmañ ca dīpanastvāmapācanaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.24"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.24</label>
       elātagarakuṣṭhamāṃsīdhyāmakatvapattranāgapuṣpapriyaṅguhareṇukāvyāghranakhaśukticaṇḍāsthauṇeyaka
      śrīveṣṭakacorakavālakaguggulusarjjarasaturuṣkakundurukāguruspṛkkābhadradārukuṅkumāni
      punnāgakesarañceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.25"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.25</label>
       elādiko vātakapho nihanyād viṣam eva ca |
      <caesura/>
       varṇṇaprasādanaḥ kaṇḍūpiṭakā koṭhanāśanaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.26"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.26</label>
       vacā mustātiviṣābhadradārunāgakesarañ ceti |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.27"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.27</label>
       haridrādāruharidrākalaśīkuṭajabījāni madhukaṃ ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.28"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.28</label>
       etau vacā haridrādī gaṇau stanyaviśodhanau |
      <caesura/>
       āmātīsāraśamanau kaphamedo viśoṣaṇau |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.29"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.29</label>
       śyāmāmahāśyāmātṛvṛddantībilvakampilyakaramyakakevukaputraśreṇīgavākṣīrājavṛkṣakarañjadvaya
      guḍūcīsaptavarṇṇacchagalāntrīpīlusnuhākṣīsuvarṇṇakṣīrī ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.30"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.30</label>
       eṣa śyāmādiko nāmnā gaṇo gulmaviṣāpahaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       ānāhodarahābhedī tathodāvarttanāśanaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.31"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.31</label>
       bṛhatīkaṇṭakārikākuṭajaphalapāṭhāmadhukañceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.32"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.32</label>
       pācanīyo bṛhatyādir ggaṇaḥ pittānilāpahaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       kaphārocakakṛdrogamūtrakṛcchravināśanaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.33"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.33</label>
       paṭolācandanamūrvvāguḍūcīpāṭhā kaṭurohiṇī ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.34"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.34</label>
       paṭolādir ggaṇaḥ pittakaphārocakanāśanaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       jvaropaśamano vraṇyaś charddikaṇḍūviṣāpahaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.35"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.35</label>
       kākolīkṣīrakākolījīvakaṛṣabhakamudgaparṇṇīmedāmahāmedācchinnaruhākarkkaṭāśṛṅgītugākṣīpadmakaprapauṇḍarīka
      ṛddhivṛddhijīvantyau madhukañ ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.36"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.36</label>
       kākolyādirayam pittaśoṇitānilanāśanaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       jīvano bṛṃhaṇo vṛṣyaḥ stanyaśleṣmakaras tathā ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.37"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.37</label>
       ūṣasaindhavaśilājatukāśīsadvayahiṃgututthakañ ceti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.38.38"><label>1931 ed. 1.38.38</label>
       ūṣakādiḥ kaphaṃ hanti gaṇo medā viśoṣaṇaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       śarkkarāśmarihāmūtrakṛcchragulmapramarddanaḥ ||</l>

    <div n="39" type="adhyāya">

     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.39.1</label>
       athātaḥ saṃśodhanasaṃśamanīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.2"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.39.3</label>
       madanakuṭajajīmūtakekṣvākudhāmārggavakṛtavedhanalodhrasarṣapaviḍaṅgapippalīkarañjaprapūnāḍakovidārāriṣṭāśvagandhāvidulabandhumadhukajīvantī
      bimbīphalāmṛgervvāru citrasvetā śalapuṣpīvacācetyūrddhvabhāgaharāṇi || tatra
      kovidārapūrvvāṇāmphalāni | kovidārādīnām mūlāni ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.39.4</label>
       tṛvṛcchyāmādantīdravantīsaphalāviṣāṇigavākṣīcchagalāntrīpīlusnehāsuvarṇṇakṣīrīcitrakakiṇihīkuśakāsatilvakampilyakarampakapāṭalā
      pūgaharītakyāmalakavibhītakanīlinīpañcaṅgulapūtīkāragvadhamahāvṛkṣasaptacchadārkkareṇu
      jyotiṣmatī cetyadhobhāgaharāṇi ||tatra tilvakapūrvvāṇāṃ mūlāni | tilvakādīnām
      pāṭalyantānāñ ca tvacaḥ | pūgādīnām eraṇḍāntānām phalāni | pūtīkāragvadhayoḥ patrāṇi
      | śeṣāṇāṃ kṣīrāṇīti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.39.5</label>
       kośātakī saptalā devadālī karavallikā cety ubhayato bhāgaharāṇi | eṣāṃ svarasāḥ
      ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.39.6</label>
       pippalīviḍaṅgāpāmārggaśigruśirīṣasiddhārthakamaricakaravīrabimbīgirikarṇṇikākiṇihīvacājyotiṣmatīkarañjārkkalaśunātiviṣāśṛ
      ṅgaveratālīsatamālasurasārjjakeṅgudīmeṣaśṛṅgīmātuluṅgīmuruṅgīpīlujātīsālatālamadhūkalākṣāhiṃgulavaṇamadyagośakṛdrasomūtrāṇi
      śirovirecanāni | tatra karavīrapūrvvāṇām phalāni | tālīsapūrvvāṇāṅ kandāḥ |
      tālīsakādīnāmarjjakāntānām patrāṇi | iṅgudīmeṣaśṛṅgyos tvak |
      mātuluṅgīmuruṅgīpīlujātīnām puṣpāṇi | śālatālamadhūkānāṃ sārāḥ | lākṣāhiṃgu ca
      niryāsau | lavaṇāni pārthivaviśeṣāḥ | madyam āsutasaṃyogāḥ | śakṛdrasamūtre malāviti
      ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.39.7</label>
       saṃśamanāni ata urdhvvam vakṣyāmaḥ || tatra
      bhadradārukuṣṭhaharidrāvaruṇameṣaśṛṅgībalātibalārttagalakacchurāśallakīkuberākṣīvīratarasahacarāgnimanthavatsādanīśva
      daṃṣṭrāśmabhedakārkkālarkkaśatāvarīpunarnnavāsukavasirakāñcanabhārggīvṛścikālīvadarayavakulattaprabhṛtīni
      dve cādye pañcamūlyau samāsena vātasaṃ śamano varggaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.39.8</label>
       candanahrīverośīramañjiṣṭhāpayasyāgundraśevālakahlārakotpalamūrvvāprabhṛtīni
      nyagrodhādirutpalādiriti samāsena pittasaṃśamano vargaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.39.9</label>
       kāleyakāgurutailaparṇṇikākuṣṭhaharidrāśītaśivāśatapuṣpāsaralārāsnāprakīryodakīceṅgudīsumanāḥ
      kākādanīlāṅgalakīhastiparṇṇamuñjālalāmajja kaprabhṛtīnivallīkaṇṭakapañcamūlyau dve
      pippalyādir mmuṣkakādir vvacādiḥ surasādirāragvadhādir utpalādir iti samāsena
      śleṣmasaṃśamano varggaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.39.10</label>
       tatra sarvvāṇy evauṣadhāni vyādhagnipuruṣabalānyevekṣya vidadhyād vyādhyabalād
      adhikam auṣadham upayuktan tam upasāmyavyādhim anyamāvahati || agnyabalād adhikam
      ajīrṇṇam viṣṭabhya vā pacyate | puruṣabalād adhikaṃ glānimūrcchanā vahati | śamanam
      evaṃ saṃśodhanam atipātayati | hīnam ebhyo dattam akiñcitkaram bhavati | tasmāt
      samam eva vidhyāt ||</l>



     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.39.11</label>
       bhavati cātra ||
      <caesura/>
       roge śodhanasādhye tu yam vidyād doṣam ulvanaṃ
      <caesura/>
       taṃ samīkṣya bhiṣak kuryād doṣapacyāvanaṃ mṛduḥ ||</l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.11.1"><label>1.39.11.1</label>
       jaloddhṛtauṣadhapalas toyadvikuḍavāyutaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       pādāvaśeṣitaḥ kvāthaḥ pūtaḥ pānāya śasyate ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.11.2"><label>1.39.11.2</label>
       tadvat kṣīrārddhakuḍavaḥ sauṣadhastriguṇodakaḥ ||
      <caesura/>
       kalkākṣamātrikaś cūrṇṇo biḍālapadakānvitaḥ ||<anchor n="SS.1.39.11.2-n1"/></l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.11.3"><label>1.39.11.3</label>
       bhavet pāṇitalaṃ lehaḥ svarasas tu paladvayaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       vyādhyādīnām bale madhye mātraiṣā śamanauṣadhai ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.11.4"><label>1.39.11.4</label>
       ato jñātveṣṭato yojyo hīmahī nādhikedhikāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       jñātvā koṣṭhauṣadhabalam mātrākalpyā suśobhane ||</l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.39.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.39.12</label>
       cale doṣe mṛdau koṣṭhe nekṣan tatra balan nṛṇāṃ |
      <caesura/>
       avyāpaddurbbalasyāpi<anchor n="SS.1.39.12-n1"/> śodhanaṃ hi tadā bhavet || </l>

    <div n="40" type="adhyāya">
     <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 40, draft based on MS H]</head>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.1</label>
       athāto dravyarasavīryavipākavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.2"/>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.3</label>
       kecid ācāryā vruvate | dravyam pradhānam kasmāt vyavasthitatvāt | iha khalu dravyam
      vyavasthitan na rasādayaḥ | yathā ye phale rasādayas te pakve na bhavanti ||
      nityatvāc ca nityaṃ hi dravyam anityaṃ hi guṇāḥ | yathā kalkādi pravibhāgās tad eva
      sampannarasagandhaṃ vyāpannarasagandhavān bhavatīti | svajātivyavasthānāc ca yathā
      pārthivaṃ dravyam anyabhāvan na gacchati | evaṃ śoṣāṇi | pañcendriyagrahaṇāc ca |
      pañcaindriyair gṛhyate draṣṭavyan na rasādayaḥ | āśrayatvāc ca dravyam āśritārasā
      iti | ārambha sāmarthyāc ca dravyāśrita ārambhaḥ || yathā vidārigandhādim āhṛtyāv
      adya vipaced ity evam ādiṣu na rasādiṣ ārambhaḥ | śāstraprāmāṇyāc ca śāstraṃ ha |
      dvividhan dravyaṃ sthāvarañ jañgam ti | kramāpekṣikatvāc ca rasādīnāṃ rasādayo hi
      dravyakramam apekṣante yathā taruṇe taruṇāḥ | saṃpūrṇa sampūrṇā iti |
      ekadeśasādhyatvāc ca dravyāṇām ekadeśenāpi vyādhayaḥ sādhyante | yathā
      mahāvṛkṣakṣīreṇeti | tasmād dravyam pradhānan rasādayaḥ kasmāt niravayavatvāt
      dravyasya | dravyalakṣaṇan tu kriyāguṇasamavāyaḥ kriyādravye vidyate | guṇāḥ
      samavāyakāraṇañ ceti ||</l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.4</label>
       nety āhur anye rasās tu pradhānan kasmāt āgamāt āgamo hi śāstram ity ucyate |
      śāstre rasā adhikṛtā yathā rasāyatta āhāra iti | upadeśāc ca | upadiśyate hi | yathā
      madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaṃ śamayanti | ato rasāḥ pradhānaṃ | anumāc ca | rasato hy
      anumīyate dravyaṃ | yathā madhuram iti || ṛṣivacanāc ca | ṛṣivacano vedaḥ | yathā
      kiñcid ījyārtham madhuram āhared iti | tasmāt rasāḥ pradhānaṃ | raseṣu tu guṇasaṃjñā
      rasalakṣaṇam atropadekṣyāmaḥ | </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.5</label>
       nety āhur anye vīryam pradhānam iti | kasmāt prādhānyāt | ihatvauṣadhakarmmāṇi
      vīrya prādhānyaṃ na bhavanti | tad yathā | urddhabhāgodhobhāgobhayabhāgasaṃśamanaṃ
      sāṅgrāhikadīpanalekhanavṛṃhaṇarasāyanavājīkaraṇaś ca
      yathuharavilayanadāraṇamarddanaprāṇaghnaviṣapraśamanāni vīrya prādhānyena bhavanti |
      tantu vīryaṃ dvividhaṃ | uṣṇaṃ śītaṃ cāgniṣomīyatvāj jagataḥ | kecid aṣṭavidham āhuḥ
      | uṣṇaṃ śītaṃ snigdhaṃ rūkṣam vi ṣadam piccilam mṛdus tīkṣṇañ ceti | etāni khalu
      vīryāṇi svabhāvaguṇotkarṣād rasam abhibhūyātmakarmma kurvvanti | yathā tāvad
      vṛhatyañ ca mūlaṅ kaṣāya tiktaṃ vātaṃ śamayaty uṣṇavīryatvāt | kaṭukā pippalīpittaṃ
      śamayati | mṛduśītavīryatvāt | tiktā kākamācī pittaṃ varddhayaty uṣṇavīryatvāt |
      kaṭukaṃ mūlaṃ śleṣmāṇaṃ varddhayati snigdhavīryatvāt | amlaṃ kapitthaṃ śleṣmāṇaṃ ti
      rukṣavīryatvāt || bha || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.6</label>
       ye rasā vātaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
      <caesura/>
       rukṣalāghavaśaity āni na te hanyuḥ samīraṇam || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.7</label>
       ye rasāḥ pittaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣuvai |
      <caesura/>
       taikṣṇyauṣṇyalaghutā caiva na te talkarmmakāriṇaḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.8</label>
       ye rasāḥ śleṣmaśamanā bhavanti yadi teṣu vai |
      <caesura/>
       snehagauravaśaity ānu na te tatkarmmakāriṇaḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.9</label>
       tasmād vīryaṃ pradhānam iti || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.10</label>
       nety āhur anye vipākaḥ pradhānam iti | kasmāt samyaṅ mithyā vipakvatvāt | iha hi
      dravyāṇyapaha tāni samyaṅ mithyā cāvipakvāni guṇan doṣam vā janayaṃti | tatrāhur
      anye prati ra sampāka iti | vipākaḥ kecit trividham icchanti | madhuram amlam
      kaṭukañceti | tat tu na samyak | bhūtaguṇād āgamāc cāmlo vipāko nāsti | pittaṃ hi
      vidagdham amlatām upaity āgneyatvāt | yad evaṃ lavaṇo 'pyanyaḥ pāke bhaviṣyati |
      śleṣmā hi vidagdho lavaṇatām upaiti | tamādasiddhānta eṣaḥ | pratirasam
      amlāmlasyaivaṃ sarvvaṣām iti dṛṣṭāntañ codāharanti | yathā śāliyavamudgādayaḥ
      prakīrṇāḥ svabhāvam uttarakāle pi na parity ajanti tadvat iti | kecit punar
      avalavanto valavatāṃ vaśamāyānt it evam avasthitaḥ pāka iti | āgame svāha | dvividha
      eva pāko madhuraḥ kaṭukaś ca | tayor madhurākhyo guruḥ kaṭukākhyo laghur iti | tatra
      pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśānāṃ dvaividhyam bhavati | guṇasādharmyān gurutā | laghutā ca
      pṛthivyā yo gurvyaḥ | śeṣāṇi laghūni tasmād dvividha eva pāko bhavati || bha ||</l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.11</label>
       dravyeṣu pacyamāneṣu yeṣv amvupṛthivīguṇāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       nivarttante 'dhikās tatra pāko madhura ucyate || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.12</label>
       tejonilākāśaguṇāḥ pacyamāneṣu yeṣu tu |
      <caesura/>
       nivarttante 'dhikās tatra pākaḥ kaṭuka ucyate || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.13</label>
       pṛthak tvavādināmeṣeva vādinām vādasaṃgrahaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       caturṇṇām api sāmagryam icchantyatra vipaścitaḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.14</label>
       tad dravyam ātmanā kiñcit kiñcid vīryeṇa sevitaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       kiñcid rasavipākābhyān doṣaṃ hanti karoti vā || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.15</label>
       pāko nāsti vinā vīryād vīryan nāsti vinā rasāt |
      <caesura/>
       raso nāsti vinā dravyād dravyaṃ śreṣṭhatamaṃ smṛtaṃ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.16"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.16</label>
       janman tu dravyarasayor anyonyāpekṣikaṃ smṛtaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       anyonyāpekṣikaṃ janma yathā syād dehadehinoḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.17</label>
       vīryasaṃjñā guṇā ye 'ṣṭau te 'pi dravyāśrayāḥ smṛtāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       raseṣu na bhavantyete nirguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.18</label>
       dravye dravye ca yasmāddhi vipacyante na ṣaḍ rasāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       śreṣṭhaṃ dravyamato jñeyaṃ śeṣā bhāvās tadāśrayāḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.19</label>
       amīmāṃsyānyacintyāni prasiddhāni svabhāvataḥ |
      <caesura/>
       āgamenopayojyāni bheṣajāni vicakṣaṇaiḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.20</label>
       pratyakṣalakṣaṇaphalās prasiddhāś ca svabhāvataḥ |
      <caesura/>
       oṣadhīn hetubhir vvidvān na parīkṣet kathañcana || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.40.21</label>
       sahastreṇāpi hetūnān nāmvaṣṭhādir virecayet |
      <caesura/>
       tasmāt tiṣṭhed vimatimānāgameśa tu hetuṣu || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.21.1"><label>1.40.21.1</label>
       yā svabhāvavijñānaṃ vā raśaṃ yuktasenikaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       āturopakramam miśraṃ bhūmijñānan tathaiva ca || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.21.2"><label>1.40.21.2</label>
       dravyasaṃgrahaṇañ caiva tathā śamanaśodhanaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       rasavīryavipākena proktam anyad daśaiva tu || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.40.trailer"> caturthodaśa || || || </l>


    </div>

    <div n="41" type="adhyāya">
     <head>[Adhyāya 41]</head>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.41.1</label>
       athāto dravyaviśeṣavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.2"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.41.3</label>
       tatra pṛthivyaptejovāyvākāśānāṃ samudāyād dravyābhinirvṛttir bbhavati | idaṃ
      pārthivam idam apyam idan tejasam idam vāyavyam idam ākāśyam iti || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.1"><label>1.41.4.1</label>
       tatra sthūla<pc> </pc>sāndra<pc> </pc>manda<pc> </pc>sthira<pc> </pc>guru<pc
       > </pc>kaṭhina<pc> </pc>gaṃdha<pc> </pc>guṇa<pc> </pc>bahulam īṣatkaṣāyaprāyaso
      madhuram iti pārthivan tat sthairya<pc> </pc>gaurava<pc
       > </pc>saṃghātopacaya<pc> </pc>karaṃ viśeṣataś cādhogatisvabhāvam iti || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.2"><label>1.41.4.2</label>
       śīta<pc> </pc>stimita<pc> </pc>manda<pc> </pc>guru<pc> </pc>rasa<pc> </pc>sāndra<pc> </pc>mṛdu<pc> </pc>picchila<pc> </pc>rasa<pc> </pc>guṇa<pc> </pc>bahulam
      īṣadamlaṃ prāyaso madhuram āpyan tat snehanahlādanaviṣyandanakaram iti | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.3"><label>1.41.4.3</label>
       tīkṣṇoṣṇarūkṣasūkṣmalaghuviṣadaṃ rūpaguṇabahulam īṣadamlaprāyam viśeṣataś
      corddhvagatisvabhāvam iti taijasaṃ ||
      taddahanapacanatāpanaprakāśanaprabhāvarṇṇakaram iti | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.4"><label>1.41.4.4</label>
       sūkṣmarūkṣakharaśiśiralaghuviṣadaṃ sparśaguṇabahulam īṣattiktam viśeṣataḥ kaṣāyam
      iti vāyavyaṃ tadvaiṣadyaṃ lāghavaglapanavirūkṣaṇakaram iti || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.4.5"><label>1.41.4.5</label>
       ślakṣṇasūkṣmavyavāyiviṣadaviviktarasaṃ śabdaguṇabahulam ākāśyan tasmāt tat
      mārddavasauṣiryalāghavakaram iti || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.41.5</label>
       anena nidarśanena nānauṣadhabhūtañ jagati kiñcid dravyam astīti kṛtvā tan taṃ
      yuktiviśeṣamarthañ cābhipratītya svavīryaguṇayuktāni dravyāṇi kārmmukāni<anchor
       n="SS.1.41.5-n1"/> bhavanti || tāni yadā kurvvanti sa kālaḥ | yat kurvanti tat
      karmma | yena kurvvanti tad vīryaṃ | yatra kurvvanti tad adhikaraṇaṃ | yathā
      kurvvanti sa upāyaḥ | yad abhiniṣpādayanti tat phalam iti | </l>

     <ab corresp="#SS.1.41.5" type="apparatus">
      <list type="notes">
       <item corresp="#SS.1.41.5-n1">The word <foreign>kārmuka</foreign> is known in early
        medical texts from this instance and one in the <title>Carakasaṃhitā</title>
        1.26.13. The word is formed by P.5.1.103 in the sense “capable of accomplishing an
        action."</item>
      </list>
     </ab>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.41.6</label>
       tad atra virecanadravyāṇy ambupṛthivīguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni | pṛthivyāpo hi gurvvyaḥ |
      gurutvād adho gacchanti | tasmād virecanadravyāṇy ambupṛthivīguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni |
      vamanadravyāṇy agnivāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhāni | agnivāyū hi laghū laghutvāc corddhvam
      uttiṣṭhataḥ | tasmād vamanaprāmāṇyād agnivāyubhūyiṣṭhāny ubhayaguṇabhūyiṣṭhan
      dravyam ubhayato bhāgaharaṃ | ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ saṃśamanaṃ | sāṃgrāhikam
      anilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ | dīpanam agniguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ | lekhanam anilānalaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ
      | bṛṃhanam pṛthivyambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ | evam auṣadhakarmmāṇy anumānāt sādhayet || </l>



     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.41.7</label>
       bhavanti ślokāḥ ||
      <caesura/>
       mahyambvagnyātmakair ddravyais tribhiḥ sāmyati mārutaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       khabhūmyambuvāyujaiḥ pittañ caturbbhiḥ saṃpraśāmyati || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.41.8</label>
       kaphaḥ khatejo'nilajais tribhiḥ śāmyati dehināṃ |
      <caesura/>
       khavāyuktābhyān dravyābhyāṃ vṛddhim abhyeti mārutaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.41.9</label>
       āgneyam eva yad dravyan tena pittam udīryate |
      <caesura/>
       mahyambujābhyān dravyābhyāṅ kaphaś cābhivivarddhate || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.41.10</label>
       evam eva guṇādhikyaṃ dravye dravye vyavasthitaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       dviśo vā bahuśo vāpi jñātvā doṣe 'vacācaret || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.41.11</label>
       tatra ya ime guṇāṣṭauvīryasaṃjñakāḥ | śītoṣṇasnigdharūkṣamṛdutīkṣṇapicchilaviṣadās
      teṣān tīkṣṇoṣṇāv āgneyau | śītapicchilāv ambuguṇabhūyiṣṭhau |
      pṛthivīsomaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaḥ | snehas toyākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ | mṛdutvaṃ |
      vāyuguṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ raukṣyaṃ | kṣitisamīraṇabhūyiṣṭhaṃ vaiṣadyaṃ | vipākāv uktaguṇau
      | karmmāṇy uṣṇasya dahanapācanamūrcchanasvedanavamanavirecanāni || śītasya
      prahlādanaviṣkambhanasthirīkaraṇaprasādanakledanajīvanāni | snigdhasya
      snehanabṛṃhaṇasantarppaṇavyājīkaraṇavayaḥsthāpanāni ||
      rūkṣasyānilavṛddhisaṃgrahaṇapīḍanavirūkṣaśoṣarohaṇāni || viṣadasya
      kledāvūṣaṇavirūkṣaśoṣarohaṇāni ||
      picchilasyopalepanapūraṇabṛṃhaṇasaṃśleṣaṇavyājīkaraṇāni || mṛdo raktamān
      saprasādanamukhyasaṃsparśanāni || tīkṣṇasya saṅgrahācūṣaṇāvadāraṇaśrāvaṇāni |
      tatroṣṇasnigdhau vātaghnau | śītamṛdupicchilāḥ pittaghnāḥ | tīkṣṇarūkṣaviṣadāḥ
      śleṣmaghnāḥ | gurupāko vātapittaghnaḥ | laghupākaḥ śleṣmapittaghna iti | teṣu
      mṛduśītoṣṇāḥ sparśagrāhyāḥ | picchilaviṣadau cakṣuḥsparśābhyāṃ | snigdharūkṣau
      cakṣuṣā | tīkṣṇaḥ sukhaduḥkhotpādanāt | gurupākaḥ sṛṣṭaviṇmūtratayā kaphāṃ kleśanañ
      ca | laghur bbaddhaviṇmūtratayā mārutakopanañ ca | tatra tulyaguṇeṣu bhūteṣu
      rasavaiśeṣyam upalakṣayet || yathā madhuro guruś ca pārthivaḥ | madhurasnigdhaśītāś
      cāpyā iti || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.41.12</label>
       || bhavati cātra || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.41.12i"><label>1.41.12i</label>
       guṇā ye uktā dravyeṣu śarīreṣv api tān viduḥ |
      <caesura/>
       sthānavṛddhikṣayāt tasmād dehināṃ dravyahetukā iti || </l>

    <div n="42" type="adhyāya">

     <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 42, draft based on MS H]</head>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.42.1</label>
       athāto rasaviśeṣavi-jñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.42.3</label>
       ākāśapavanadahanatoyabhūmiṣu yathāsaṅkhyam ekottaraparivṛddhāḥ || śa
      bdasparśarūparasagandhāḥ || tasmād āpyo rasaḥ parasparānupraveśāc ca sarvveṣāṃ
      sānnidhyam asti utkarṣāt tu grahaṇaṃ | sa khalvāpyo rasaḥ
      śeṣabhūtasaṃsarggādvidagdhaḥ ṣaḍvidho bhavati | tad yathā | madhuro 'mlo lavaṇaḥ
      kaṭukastiktaḥ kaṣāya iti | tatrodakavāhulyātmadhuraḥ | toyāgnivāhulyādamlaḥ
      bhūmyagnivāhulyāl lavaṇaḥ vāyvākāśavāhulyāttiktaḥ | vāyvagnivāhulyātkaṭukaḥ
      pṛthivyanilavāhulyātkaṣāya iti || </l>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.42.4</label>
       tatra madhurāmlalavaṇā vātaghnāḥ | madhuratiktakaṣāyāḥ pittaghnāḥ kaṭutiktakaṣāyāḥ
      śleṣmaghnāḥ || </l>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.42.5</label>
       tatra vāyurātmaivātmā | pittamāgneyaṃ | śleṣma saumya iti || </l>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.42.6</label>
       ta ete rasāḥ svayonivardhanā anyayonipraśamanāś ca | </l>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.42.7</label>
       kecid āhur agnīṣomīyatvājjagataḥ | dvividhā rasāḥ saumyā āgneyāś ca | tatra
      madhuratiktakaṣāyāḥ saumyāḥ dvividhā kaṭvamlalavaṇā āgneyāḥ | madhurāmlalavaṇāḥ
      snigdhā guravaś ca dvividhā kaṭutiktakaṣāyā rūkṣā laghavaś ca | saumyāḥ śītāḥ |
      āgneyās tūṣṇāḥ | </l>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.1"><label>1.42.8.1</label>
       tatra śaityarūkṣalāghavavaiṣadyaguṇalakṣaṇo vāyuḥ | tasya samānayoniḥ kaṣāyo rasaḥ
      | saumyaḥ śaityāc chaity am abhivardhayati | raukṣyād raukṣyaṃ lāghavāl lāghavaṃ
      vaiṣadyād vaiṣadyam iti || </l>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.2"><label>1.42.8.2</label>
       auṣṇyataikṣṇyaraukṣyalāghavavaiṣadyaguṇalakṣaṇampittantasya samānayoniḥ kaṭuko
      rasaḥ | saumya auṣṇyād auṣṇyam abhivardhayati | taikṣṇyāt taikṣṇyaṃ raukṣyād
      raukṣyaṃ lāghavāl lāghavaṃ vaiśadyād vaiśadyam iti || </l>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8.3"><label>1.42.8.3</label>
       mādhuryasnehagauravaśaityapaicchilyaguṇalakṣaṇaḥ śleṣmā tasya samānayo nirmadhuro
      rasaḥ | saumya mādhuryāt mādhuryam abhivardhayati | snehāt snehaṃ gauravād gauravaṃ
      śaityāc chaityaṃ paicchilyāt paicchilyam iti ||</l>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.42.8</label>
       tasya punar vviparītaḥ kaṭuko rasaḥ | śleṣmaṇaḥ pratyanīkatvāt | kaṭukyātmādhuryam
      abhibhavati | raukṣyāt snehaṃ lāghavād gauravaṃ auṣṇyāt paicchity an tad etan
      nidarśanamātram uktaṃ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.42.9</label>
       rasalakṣaṇam ata ūrdhvaṃ vakṣyāmaḥ || tatra yaḥ paritoṣam utpādayati tarppayati
      mukhopalepañ janayati prahlādayati śleṣmāṇañ cābhivardhayati sa madhuraḥ || yo
      dantaharṣam utpādayati | mukhāśrāvañ jana-yati śraddhāñ cotpādayati so 'mlaḥ || yo
      bhaktarucim utpādayati | kaphaprasekañ janayati mārddavañ copādayati sa lavaṇaḥ ||
      yo jihvām udvejayati śiro gṛhṇāti nāsikāñ ca śrāvayati sa kaṭukaḥ || yo gale śoṣam
      utpāda-yati mukhavaiṣadyam utpādayati bhaktaruciñ copādyati sa tiktaḥ || ya āsyam
      pariśoṣayati- jihvāṃ stambhayati kaṇṭham badhnāti hṛdayam pīḍayati sa kaṣāyaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.1"><label>1.42.10.1</label>
       rasaguṇān ata ūrdhvam vakṣyāmaḥ || tatra madhuro raso raktamāṃsado 'sthimajjojaḥ
      śukravardhanaś cākṣuṣyaḥ keśyauvalakṛtsandhānaḥ śoṇitaḥ śoṇitaprasādo
      vālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇahitaḥ ṣaṭpadapipīlikānāmiṣṭatamaḥ || tṛṣṇāmūrcchādāhaḥ
      praśamanaḥ | ṣaḍindriyaprasādanaś ceti | sa evaṃguṇo 'py eka evātyartham
      upayujyamānaḥ kāsaḥ śvāso lasakavamathurvvadanamādhuryasvaropaghātakṛmigalagaṇḍān
      āpādayati | tathārvvudaślīpadavastigudopalepābhiṣyandaprabhṛtīn nayanavikārānn
      upajayati || </l>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.2"><label>1.42.10.2</label>
       amlas tu jaraṇaḥ pācanapavananigrahaṇo nulomano vidāhī vahiḥśītaḥ kledanaḥ prāyaśo
      hṛdyaś ceti | sa khalv evaṃguṇo 'py eka evātyartham upayujyamāno
      dantaharṣanayanasammīlanaromasamvejanakaphavilāyanaśarīrapraśithilatām āpādayati |
      tathā
      kṣatavihatadagdhadaṣṭabhagnaśū-nacyutāvamathitacchiyavisarppitacchinnaviddhotpiṣṭādīni
      pāca-yaty āgneyasvabhāvatvvāt || </l>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.3"><label>1.42.10.3</label>
       lavaṇas tu saṃśodhanaḥ pācano viśleṣaṇas tarppaṇaḥ kledanaḥ śaithilyakṛt
      sarvvarasapratyanīkabhūto mārggaviśodhanaḥ sarvvaśarīrāvayavamārddavakaraś ceti | sa
      khalu evaṃguṇo 'py eka evātyartham upasevyamāno gātrakaṇḍūko tha śophavaivarṇṇakaraḥ
      svaropaghātendriyopatāpān upajanayati |
      tathākṣimukhapākaraktapittavātaśoṇitāmlīkāprabhṛtīnvikārān upajanayati || </l>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.4"><label>1.42.10.4</label>
       kaṭukas tu dīpanaḥ pācano rocanaḥ śodhanaḥ sthaulyā
      lyālasakaviṣakuṣṭhakaṇḍūpraśamanaḥ sandhibandhacchedano vasādanas
      stanyaśukrakaphamedasām upahantā ceti | sa khalv evaṃguṇo 'py eka evātyartham
      upayujyamāno bhramamadagalatālvoṣṭhaśoṣadāhasantāpān āpādayati | tathā
      valavighātakampatodabhedakṛt karacaraṇapārśvapṛṣṭhaprabhṛtiṣu ca vātaśūlān
      upajanayati || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.5"><label>1.42.10.5</label>
       tiktas tu rocano dīpanaḥ śodhanaḥ kaṇḍūkoṣṭhatṛṣṇāmūrcchāpraśanaḥ stanyaśodhano
      viṇmūtrakledamedovasāpūyopaśoṣaṇaś ceti | sa khalv evaṅguṇo 'py eka evātyartham
      upayujyamāno gātramanyāstambhākṣepakordditaśiraḥśūlān upa-janayati | tathā
      bhramatodabhedacchedāsyavairasyāny āpādayati || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.10.6"><label>1.42.10.6</label>
       kaṣāyas tu saṅgrāhiko ropaṇaḥ stambhanaḥ śodhanollekhanaḥ śoṣaṇaḥ pīḍanaḥ
      kledopaśoṣaṇaś ceti | sa khalv evaṅguṇo 'py eka evātyartham upayujyamāno
      hṛdayapīḍāsyaśoṣodarādhmānavākyagrahamanyāstambhaprabhṛtīn vikārān upajanayati |
      tathā gātrasphuraṇacimicimāyanākuñcanākṣepaṇaprabhṛtīn vikārānupajanayati || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.42.11</label>
       sarvveṣām eva dravyāṇy upadekṣyāmaḥ | tad yathā kākolyādi
      kṣīraghṛtavasāmajjaśāliyavagodhūmamāṣaśṛṅgāṭakakaśeruka
      kālāṅkālukapiyālapuṣkaravījakāśmaryamadhūkadrākṣākharjūrarājādananālikerekṣuvikārāḥ
      | balātibalātmaguptāvidārīpayasyāgokṣurakakṣīramoraṭamadhūlikākūṣmāṇḍādiḥ samāsena
      madhuro varggaḥ ||
      dāḍimāmalakamātuluṅgāmrāmrātakakapitthakaramarddavadaraprācīnāmalakakośāmrabhavyapārāvatavetraphalatintiḍīkalajacāmlavetasadantaśaṭhadadhitakrasurāsauvīratuṣodakadhānyāmlaprabhṛtīni
      samāsenāmlo varggaḥ ||
      saindhavasauvarccalaviḍapākyaromakasāmudrapācimakṣāroṣarasuvarccilaprabhṛtīni
      samāsena lavaṇo varggaḥ || pippa-lyādiḥ surasādir
      mmadhuśigrumūlakalaśunasumukhaśītaśivakuṣṭhadevadāruhareṇukā
      'valgujaphalacaṇḍāguggulumustalāṅgalakīśukanāsīpīluprabhṛtī-ni śālasārādiś ca
      prāyaśaḥ kaṭuko varggaḥ ||
      āragvadhādirgguḍūcyādirmmaṇḍūkaparṇṇīvetrakarīraharidrādvayendrayavavaruṇasvādukaṇṭakasaptaparṇṇavṛhatīdvayaśaṃkhinītṛvṛtkṛtavedhanakarkkoṭakakāravellavārttākukaravīrasumanāḥśaṃkhapuṣpyapāmārggatrāyamāṇāśokarohivaijayantīsuvarccalāvṛścikālījyotiṣmatīprabhṛtīni
      tikto varggaḥ || nyagrodhādirambaṣṭhādir lodhrādiḥ priyaṅvādistriphalā
      śallakījamvvasthitindukādīni katakaśākaphalāni sālasārādiś ca prāyasaḥ
      kuravakakovidārajīvantīsuniṣaṇṇakaprabhṛtīni varakādayo mudgādayaś ca samāsena
      kaṣā-yo varggaḥ || </l>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.42.12</label>
       tatraiteṣāṃ rasānāṃ saṃyogās triṣaṣṭirv bhavanti || tad yathā pañcadaśa dvikāḥ |
      viṃśatis trikāḥ | pañcadaśa catuṣkāḥ | ṣaṭ pañcakāḥ | ekaṣaṭkāḥ | ekaikaśaś ca
      śaḍrasā iti | teṣām anyatra vakṣyāmaḥ || </l>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.42.13</label>
       bhavati cātra ||
      <caesura/>
       yuktāḥ ṣaḍadhigacchanti valino vaśyatāṃ rasāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       yathā doṣāḥ prakupitā vaśaṃ yānti valīyasa iti ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.42.trailer"> || 42 ||</l>



    </div>

    <div n="43" type="adhyāya">
     <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 43, draft based on MS H]</head>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.43.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.43.1</label>
       athāto vamanadravyavikalpavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.part1"><label>1.43.3.part1</label>
       vamanadravyānām phalākhyānām madhye madanaphalāni śreṣṭhatamāni bhavanti || tatra
      madanapuṣpāṇām ātapaśuṣkāṇā cūrṇaprakuñcaṃ pratyak puṣpīnimvakaṣāyāṇām anyatamenālo
      pāyayitvā vāmayet | madanaśatvāṭūcūrṇṇāny evam madhulavaṇayuktāny abhiprataptāni |
      madanaśalāṭucūrṇṇasiddhām vā tilayavāgūn | nivṛttām vā nātihariti pāṇḍūnāṃ
      kuśamūḍhāvavaddhamṛdgomayapraliptānāṃ
      yavavūsamāṣaśālyādidhānyarāśāvaṣṭharātroṣitaklinnabhinnānām phalapippalīrāhṛtyātape
      pariśoṣayet tāsāṃ dadhipalavimṛditapariśuṣkāṇāṃ subhājanasthānām antarnnakhamuṣṭhim
      uṣṇena yaṣṭhīmadhukaṣāyeṇa kovidārādhyanyatamakāṣāyeṇa vā vimṛdya trirātraparyuṣitam
      madhusaindhavayuktam āśīrbhir abhimantritam udaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukham āturam pāyayet
      anena mantreṇa abhimantrya ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.1"><label>1.43.3.1</label>
       brahmadakṣāśvirūdrendrabhūcandrārkkānilānalāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       ṛṣayaḥ sauṣadhigrāmā bhūtasaṃghāś ca pāntu te || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.2"><label>1.43.3.2</label>
       rasāyaneva siddhānān devānām amṛtaṃ yathā |
      <caesura/>
       sudhevottamanāgānāsbhaiṣajyam idam astu te ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.43.3.part2"><label>1.43.3.part2</label>
       viśeṣeṇa śleṣmajvarapratiśyāyāntarvvidradhiṣv apravarttamāne doṣe
      pippalīvacāsarṣapakalkonmiśrair uṣṇāmvubhiḥ punaḥ punaḥ pravarttayed āsamyag
      vāntalakṣaṇād iti | madanaphalamajjacūrṇṇam vā tat kvāthaparibhāvitam vasena
      dravyakaṣāyeṇa | madanaphalamajjā siddham vā payaḥ | madanaphalamajjasiddhena vā
      payasā vā yavāgūm adhobhāgāsṛhṛdrogayoḥ | madanaphalamajjasiddhasya vā payaso
      dadhibhāvam upagatasya | dadhyuttarakaṃ dadhi vā kaphaprasekaśarddistameṣu |
      madanaphalamajjācūrṇṇa rasam vā bhallātakasenhavadādāya phāṇitībhūtaṃ lehayet |
      ātapaśuṣkam vā jīvantī kaṣāyeṇa pittakaphasthānagate | madanaphala majjākvātham vā
      pippalyādi prativāpaṃ ūṣaṇanimvakaṣāya yor anyatamena santarppaṇaṃ |
      kaphasarvvavyādhiharam iti madanaphalam uktaṃ | </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.43.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.43.4</label>
       jīmūtakakusumacūrṇṇam vā pūrvvavad eva kṣīreṇa nivṛtteṣu yavāgūṃ romaseṣu |
      santānikām vā nirllomaśeṣu | dadhyuttarakaṃ haritakapāṇḍuṣu | dadhi tat
      kaṣāyasaṃsṛṭāṃ surām vā paryāgateṣu | madanaphalamajja </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.43.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.43.5</label>
       vidhānavat kuṭajaphalamajjavidhānaṃ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.43.6"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.43.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.43.7</label>
       ikṣvākukusumacūrṇṇam vā pūrvvavad eva kṣīreṇa | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.43.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.43.8</label>
       dhāmārgavasyāpi madanaphalamajjā vidhānavad upayogaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.43.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.43.9</label>
       kṛtavedhanamadanaphalamajjapippalīmām vamanadravyaparibhāvitānām bahuśaś cūrṇṇam
      utpalādiṣu dattam āghrā ya vasati tattvanavavaddhadoṣeṣu yavāgūmākaṇṭham pītavatsu
      ca dadyād iti | śirovirecanāny evaṃ pradhānatamāni bhavanti || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.43.10"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.43.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.43.11</label>
       bhavati cātra
      <caesura/>
       kalkaiḥ kaṣāyaiḥ svarasaiś ca cūrṇṇair api ca vuddhimān |
      <caesura/>
       peyalehyādibhojyeṣu vamanānyūpakalpayet || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.43.trailer"> || 43 || </l>


    </div>

    <div n="44" type="adhyāya">

     <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 44, draft based on MS H]</head>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.1</label>
       athāto virecanadravyavikalpavijñānīyam vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.2"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.3</label>
       aruṇābhan tṛvṛn mūlaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ mūlavirecane |
      <caesura/>
       pradhānas tilvakas tv akṣu phaleṣv api harītakī ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.4</label>
      <caesura/>
       snehāpayaḥ payassūktam iti prādhānyasaṅgrahaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       teṣām vidhānaṃ vakṣyāmi yathāvad anupūrvvaśaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.5</label>
       vairecanadravyakaṣāyapītam mūlam
      <caesura/>
       mahattraivṛtamatra śuddhaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       cūrṇṇīkṛtaṃ saindhavanāgarāḍhyam
      <caesura/>
       pibet tad amlair anilādhijuṣṭaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.6</label>
       svādukvāthair api cekṣor vvikāraiḥ paitteroge kṣīrayuktān nihanyāt |
      <caesura/>
       drākṣārasatriphalākvāthamūtrair yuktam pibet kaphajavyoṣagāḍhaṃ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.7</label>
       trivarṇṇakatrikaṭukābhyānyuktaṃ lihyāc cūrṇṇan tadguḍenābhiyojyaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       kvāthaprasthe kuḍavan tasya dadyāt yuktyā dadyān nāgaraṃ saindhavañ ca ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.8</label>
       pacet sarvvaṃ yāvadetad ghanaṃ syāl lehībhūtan tatprayojyaṃ tatas tu |
      <caesura/>
       tṛvṛtkalkonāgarārddhena yuktaḥ sasaindhavo mūtrayuktastu peyaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.9</label>
       sametṛvṛn nāgare cābhayāñ ca dadyād arddham pūgaphalaṃ sadāruḥ |
      <caesura/>
       viḍaṃgasāraṃ marica vaiṣayogaḥ sasaindhavo mūtrayuktaḥ pradhānaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.10"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.11"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.12</label>
       vairecanadravyacūrṇṇasya bhāgas tataḥ kvāthaḥ sammitañcāsya tulyaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       sumardditaṃ sarppiṣā tacchritena tatkvāthośmasveditā varttitañ ca ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.13</label>
       pākaprāpte phāṇitaṃ cūrṇṇitāktaṃ kṣiptvā pakvaṃ cāvatāryā pramādāt |
      <caesura/>
       śītīkṛtvā modakaṃ saurabhājyaṅ kuryād evam bhakṣyakalpā samāsān |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.14</label>
       mudgānām vātaiḥ samaṃ sādhitānāṃ yūṣo hṛdyaḥ sadhṛtaḥ saindhavāḍhyaḥ ||
      <caesura/>
       virecayed vaidaleṣv eṣu kalpaḥ kāryās tajñair vvāmanīyeṣu caiva ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.15</label>
       ikṣur dvidhā pāṭayitvāvalipya tṛvṛt kalkaiḥ pravisandhāya cāpi |
      <caesura/>
       paktvā samyak puṭapākaṃ krameṇa khādec chītaṃ pittarogābhibhūtaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.16"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.17"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.18"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.19"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.20"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.21"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.22"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.23"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.24"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.25"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.26"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.27"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.28"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.28</label>
       vairecanikaniḥkvātha bhāgāḥ śītās trayo mitāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       dvau phāṇitasya tāṃ sarvvā nyūnaragnāvadhiśrayet ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.29"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.29</label>
       tatsādhusiddham vijñāya śītī kṛtvā nidhāpayet |
      <caesura/>
       kalaśe kṛtasaṃskāre vibhajyantu himāhimau ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.30"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.30</label>
       ūrddhvañ jātarasaṃ māsād āsavaṃ madhugandhikaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       mātrayā prapibet prātaḥ tataḥ samyag viricyate ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.31"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.31</label>
       vairecanikamūlānāṃ kvāthe māsān susādhitān |
      <caesura/>
       sudhautaṃ tatkaṣāyeṇa śālīnāñ cāpi taṇḍulaṃ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.32"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.32</label>
       avakṣudyaikataḥ piṇḍāṃ kṛtvā śuṣkāṃ sucūrṇṇitāṃ |
      <caesura/>
       śālitaṇḍulacūrṇṇantu samyak svinnaṃ suśītalaṃ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.33"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.33</label>
       tasya piṣṭasya bhāgām̐strīn kiṇvabhāgavimiśritān |
      <caesura/>
       maṇḍodakārthe kvāthan tu dadyāt tat sarvam ekataḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.34"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.34</label>
       nidadhyāt kalase tāntu surāñ ca tarasām pibet |
      <caesura/>
       eṣa eva surākalpo vamaneṣv api kīrttitaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.35"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.35</label>
       mūlāni tṛvṛtādīnām prathamasya gaṇasya ca |
      <caesura/>
       mahataḥ pañcamūlasya bhārggī śārṅgaṣvayor api ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.36"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.36</label>
       triphalām vacām ativiṣāṃ sudhāhemavatīn tathā |
      <caesura/>
       saṃhṛtyaitāni sarvvāṇi kuryād bhāgāvubhau pṛthak ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.37"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.37</label>
       kuryān niḥkvātham ekasmin ekasmin cūrṇṇam eva ca |
      <caesura/>
       tena kvāthena bahuśo viśuddhāṃ bhāvayed yavān ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.38"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.38</label>
       śuṣkāṇām mṛdubhṛṣṭānān teṣām bhāgās trayo mitāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       caturtham bhāgam āvāpya cūrṇṇam apyatra kīrttitaṃ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.39"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.39</label>
       kalase prakṣiyedvidvān tatas tan tadanantaraṃ |
      <caesura/>
       teṣām eva kaṣāyeṇa śītenābhiprapūrayet ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.40"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.40</label>
       pūrvvavat sannidadhyāt tu jñeyaṃ sauvīrakaṃ hitaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       pūrvvokta varggam āhṛtya dvidhā kṛtvaikam etayoḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.41"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.41</label>
       bhāgaṃ saṃkṣudya saṃsṛjya yavaiḥ sthālyāṃ sahākṣipet |
      <caesura/>
       ajaśṛgyāḥ kaṣāyeṇa tenābhyāsicya sādhayet ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.42"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.42</label>
       susiddhāṃ cāvacāryaitām oṣadhibhyo vimokṣayet |
      <caesura/>
       vimṛdya satuṣān etān tatastāṃ pūrvvavadyavāṃ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.43"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.43</label>
       pūrvvoktauṣadhabhāgasya cūrṇṇaṃ datvā |
      <caesura/>
       tenaiva sahayūṣeṇa kalase pūrvva sukṣipet ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.44"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.44</label>
       jñātvā jātarasañ cāpi tattuṣodakam āpnuyāt |
      <caesura/>
       tuṣodasauvīrakayor vvidhir eṣa prakīrttitaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.45"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.45</label>
       ṣaḍrāttrāt saptarātrād vā te ca peye sure smṛte |
      <caesura/>
       vairecaneṣu dravyeṣu tṛvṛtkalpavidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.82"><label>1.44.82</label>
       mahāvṛkṣapayaḥ pītair yavāgūstaṇḍulaiḥ kṛtāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       virecayed āśupītāguḍenotkārikā kṛtā ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.83"><label>1.44.83</label>
       leho vā sādhitaḥ samyak snuhīkṣīrasurāghṛtaiḥ |
      <caesura/>
       vibhāvitā snuhīkṣīrepippalyo lavaṇāni ca || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.84ab"><label>1.44.84ab</label>
       cūrṇṇaṅkampilyakasyāpi tat pītaṅ guḍikākṛtaṃ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.45.3"><label>1.44.45.3</label>
       cūrṇṇaṅkampilyakasyāpi tatpītaṅguḍikākṛtaṃ |</l>
