     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.62"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.63"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.64"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.64</label>
       harītakī viḍaṅgāni saindhavan nāgaran tathā ||
      <caesura/>
       marīcāni ca tat sarvvaṅ gomūtreṇa virecanaṃ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.65"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.65</label>
       harītakīm bhadradāru kuṣṭhaṃ pūgaphalan tathā ||
      <caesura/>
       saindhavaṃ śṛṅgaverañ ca gomūtreṇa virecanaṃ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.66"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.66</label>
       nīlīphalanāñ cūrṇṇantu nāgarābhayayos tathā ||
      <caesura/>
       līḍhvā guḍaiṇa salilam paś cād uṣṇam piven naraḥ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.67"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.67</label>
       pippalyādi kaṣāyeṇa pibet piṣṭāṃ harītakīṃ ||
      <caesura/>
       saindhavopahitāṃ samyag eṣa yogo virecanaḥ |</l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.69"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.70"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.71ab"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.71cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.71cd</label>
       triphalā sarvvarogaghnī ghṛtabhogena mūrcchitā ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.72ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.72</label>
       vayaḥ saṃsthāpanañ cāpi kuryāt satatasevitā |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.72cd"/>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.68"><label>1.44.68</label>
       harītakī bhakṣyamāṇā nāgareṇa guḍena vā ||
      <caesura/>
       saindhavopahitā vāpi sātatyenāgnidīpanī |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.54cd"><label>1.44.54cd</label>
       vyoṣaṃ trijātakam mustā viḍaṅgāmalake tathā ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.55"><label>1.44.55</label>
       navaitāni samānāni tṛvṛdaṣṭagāṇāni vā |
      <caesura/>
       suślakṣṇacūrṇṇitānīha gāḍitāni vimiśrayet ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.56cd"><label>1.44.56cd</label>
       ṣaḍbhiś ca śarkkarābhāgair īṣat saindhavamākṣikaiḥ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.57ab"><label>1.44.57ab</label>
       piṇḍīkṛtam bhakṣayitvātataḥ śītāmbu pāyayet ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.58cd"><label>1.44.58cd</label>
       avipattir ayaṃ yogaḥ praśastaḥ pittarogiṇāṃ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.59"><label>1.44.59</label>
       kṣārānupānam bhoktavyo vātaślemārturair nnaraiḥ ||
      <caesura/>
       bhakṣyarūpasadharmmatvād āḍhyeṣv eva vidhīyate | </l>



     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.86ef"><label>1.44.86ef</label>
       avekṣya samyag rogādīn yathāvad upayojayet ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.84cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.84cd</label>
       saptalāṃ śāṅkhinīn dantīn tṛvṛd āragvadham vacāṃ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.44.85"><label>1931 ed. 1.44.85</label>
       mūtreṇa bhāvyaṃ saptāhaṃ snuhākṣīre tathaiva ca ||
      <caesura/>
       kīrṇṇan tenāthacūrṇṇena mālyaṃ vasanam eva vā |</l>

    <div n="45" type="adhyāya">
     <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 45, draft based on MS H]</head>



     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.1</label>
       athāto dravadravyaviśeṣavijñānīyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.2"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.3</label>
       pānīyaṃm āntarīkṣyam anirddeśyarasam amṛtaṃ jīvanan tarppaṇan dhāraṇam
      āśvāsajananaṃ śramaklamapipāsāmadamūrcchātandrāpraśamanam ekāntataḥ pathyatamañ ca
      || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.4</label>
       tad evāvanau patitam anyatamam upalabhyate |
      nadīsarastaḍāgakūpavāpīpraśravaṇodbhijacauṇṭyādiṣu sthāneṣv anyatamaṃ rasam upabhate
      | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.5</label>
       tatra lohitakapilapā-ṇḍupītanīlaśukleṣv avanipradeśeṣu
      madhurāmlalavaṇakaṭutiktakaṣāyā yathāsaṃkhyam udakarasā bhavantīty eke bhāṣante || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.6</label>
       tat tu na samyak pṛthivyādīnām anyo 'nyānupraveśakṛtaḥ sa khalūdakaraso
      bhavatyutkarṣāpakarṣakṛtena saṃyogaviśeṣeṇa || tatra svalakṣaṇodakaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām
      madhuraṃ | toyāgniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām amlaṃ| pṛthivyagniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ lavaṇaṃ |
      vāyvagniguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṅ kaṭukaṃ| vāyvākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṃ tiktaṃ |
      pṛthivyanilaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyāṅ kaṣāyaṃ | ākāśaguṇabhūyiṣṭhāyām avyaktarasam avyaktaṃ
      hy ākāśam ity atas tat pradhānam avyaktarasatvāt tat peyam āntarīkṣālābhe | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.7</label>
       tatrānta-rikṣañ caturvvidhaṃ || tadyāthā | dhāraṃ kāraṃ tauṣāraṃ haimam iti | teṣān
      dhāraṃ pradhānaṃ laghutvāt tat punar dvividhaṃ | gāṅgaṃ sāmudrañ ca tayoḥ parīkṣaṇaṃ
      | tatra śālyodanapiṇḍam akuthitam avidagdhaṃ | rajatabhājanopahitaṃ varṣati deve
      kurvvīta sa cet muhūrttasthitas tādṛśa eva bhavati | tad gāṅgam iti avagantavyaṃ |
      varṇṇānyatāsitthaprakledo vā tatsāmudram iti vidyāt | tan nopādeyaṃ | sāmudram apy
      āśvayuji māsi gṛhītaṃ gāṅgavad bhavati | tad upādeyam iti |
      śuklapaṭaikadeśapracyutam athavā harmmyatalaparibhraṣṭam anyair vvā prayogair
      ggṛhītaṃ śailabhājane śailavan mṛnmaye vā pātreṣv anuguptan nidadhyāt | tat
      sarvvakālam upayuñjīta | tasyālābhe bhaumaṃ | tat punaḥ saptavidhaṃ | tad yathā
      kaupan nādeyaṃ sārasan tāḍāga m prāsravaṇam audbhijaṃ cauṇṭyam iti || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.8</label>
       tatra varṣāvarṣāsvāntarikṣamaudbhijaṃ vā seveta mahāguṇatvā-t | śaradi sarvvam
      prasannatvāt | hemante sārasan tāḍāgam vā | vasante kaupaṃ cauṇṭyaṃ prāsrāvaṇam vā |
      grīṣme 'pyevaṃ | prāvṛṣyendram anabhivṛṣṭaṃ sarvvaṃ eva | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.9</label>
       kīṭamūtrapurīṣāṇḍaśava-kothapradūṣitaṃ | tṛṇaparṇṇodakayutaṃ kaluṣam viṣasaṃyutaṃ
      || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.10</label>
       yo 'vagāheta varṣāsu pibed vāpi navañ jalaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       sa bāhyābhyantarān rogān labhate kṣipram eva tu || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.11</label>
       tatra yat paṅkaśevālatṛṇahaṭhapadmaprabhṛtibhir avacchannaṃ raviśaśikiraṇāni-lair
      vvātijuṣṭāṃ gandharasopasṛṣṭan tad vyāpannam iti vidyāt |
      sparśarasarūpagandhavīryavipākāḥ | doṣāḥ ṣaṭ kharatā paicchilyam auṣṇyaṃ
      dantagrāhitā ca sparśadoṣaḥ | paṅkasikatāśaivālavāhulyādvikṛtavarṇṇatā rūpadoṣaḥ |
      vyaktarasatā rasadoṣaḥ | aniṣṭagandhatā gandhadoṣaḥ | yad upayuktan
      tṛṣṇāgauravaśūlakaphaprasekānā-pādayati sa vīryadoṣaḥ | yad upayuktaṃ cirād
      vipacyate viṣṭambhayati sa vipākadoṣaḥ || ta ete āntarikṣe doṣā na bhavanti | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.12</label>
       vyāpanne cāgnikvathanaṃ sūryātapanam ayam piṇḍataptanirvvāpaṇam vā prasādhakam
      bhavati</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.13"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.14"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.15"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.16"/>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.17</label>
       saptakaluṣasya prasādhakāni bhvanti | tad yathā ||
      katakagomedakavisagranthiparṇṇīmūlaśevālavastrāṇimuktāmaṇiś ceti || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.19</label>
       saptaśītīkaraṇāni bhavanti | tad yathā || pravātasthāpanam dakaprakṣepanaṃ
      yaṣṭibhrāmaṇam vyajanaṃ | vastroddharaṇaṃ | vālukāprakṣepaṇaṃ sikyāvalam vanañ ceti
      || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.18</label>
       pañca nikṣepaṇāni bhavanti | tad yathā | phalakaṃ tryaṣṭakaṃ muñjāvalayaṃ dakamañ
      cikāśikyakañ ceti | </l>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.12a"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.12a</label>
       nāgapuṣpacampakotpalapāṭalāprabhṛtibhiś cādhivāsanam iti || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.20</label>
       sugandhavispaṣṭarasaṃ suśītan tarṣanāśanaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       acchaṃ laghu ca hṛdyañ ca toyaṅ guṇavad ucyate || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.21</label>
       tatra nadyaḥ paścimābhimukhāḥ pathyā laghūdakatvāt | pūrvvābhimukhā na praśasyante
      gurūdakatvāt | dakṣiṇābhimukhā nātidoṣalā bhavanti | sādhāraṇatvāt | tatra
      sahyaprabhavāḥ kuṣṭhañ janayanti | vindhyaprabhavā kuṣṭhaṃ hṛdrogañ ca |
      malayaprabhavāḥ krimīn | mahendraprabhavāḥ ślīpadodarāṇi | himavatprabhavāḥ |
      galagaṇḍaṃ kvacid gaṇḍamālāṃ | prācyāvanty āparāvantyāś cārśāṃsy upajanayanti |
      tatra pāriyātraprabhavā valārogyakarā iti || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.22"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.22</label>
       nadyaḥ śīghravahā laghvyaḥ proktā yāś cāmalodakāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       gurvvyaḥ śaivālakaluṣajalaudyāmandagāś ca yāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.23"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.24"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.24</label>
       tatra sarvveṣāṃ bhaumānām pratyūṣasi grahaṇaṃ | tatra hi śaityalāghavam adhikam
      bhavati | śaityañ cāparo guṇa iti || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.25"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.25</label>
       divārkkakiraṇair jjuṣṭaṃ juṣtam indukarair nniśi |
      <caesura/>
       arūkṣam anabhiṣyandi tattulyaṃ gaganāmbunā || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.26"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.26</label>
       gaganāmbu tridoṣaghnaṃ gṛhītaṃ yat subhājane |
      <caesura/>
       balyaṃ rasāyanaṃ śītaṃ mātrāpekṣan tataḥ paraṃ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.27ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.27ab</label>
       raktoghnaṃ śītalaṃ hlādi jvaradāhastṛṣāpahaṃ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.28"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.28</label>
       mūrcchāpittoṣmadāheṣu viṣe rakte mādatyaye ||
      <caesura/>
       bhramaklamaparīteṣu tamake vamathau tathā | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.29"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.29</label>
       ūrddhage raktapitte ca śītamambhaḥ praśasyate ||
      <caesura/>
       pārśvaśūlapratiśyāye vātaroge galagrahe | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.30"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.30</label>
       ādhmāte stimite kāṣṭhe sadyaḥśuddhe navajvare ||
      <caesura/>
       hikkāyāṃ snehapīte ca śītāmbu parivarjjayet | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.45ab"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.45cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.45cd</label>
       arocake pratiśyāye pramehaś ca yathau tathā || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.46"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.46</label>
       mande 'gnāvudare koṣṭhe jvare netrāmayeṣu ca |
      <caesura/>
       vraṇe ca madhumehe ca pānīyam mandam ācaret || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.27cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.27cd</label>
       candrakāntabhavam vāri pittaghnam vimalaṃ smṛtam | </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.33ab"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.33cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.33cd</label>
       sakṣāramprāyasaḥ kaupan nādeyaṃ kīrttitan tathā|| </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.32ab"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.32cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.32cd</label>
       tāḍākam vātalaṃ rūkṣaṃ sārasañ caiva tādṛśaṃ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.32.1"><label>1.45.32.1</label>
       autsam asmasam āśleṣāduṣṇaṃ pittena śasyate || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.35.1"><label>1.45.35.1</label>
       sarvvadā sarvvadoṣeṣu pathyam prāsrāvaṇam payaḥ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.35ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.35ab</label>
       avidāhy udbhijaṃ toyam pittaghnam madhuraṃ smṛtaṃ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.35cd"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.39ab"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.39cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.39cd</label>
       kaphamedonilaharaṃ dīpanaṃ vastiśodhanaṃ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.40ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.40ab</label>
       śvāsakāsajvaraharam pathyam uṣṇodakaṃ sadā || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.40cd"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.40.1"><label>1.45.40.1</label>
       dīpanī pācanī laghvī pathyā vastiviśodhanī |
      <caesura/>
       vātānulomanī peyākṣat pipāsaharā smṛtāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.34ab"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.34cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.34cd</label>
       kaphaghno dīpano hṛdyaḥ śuddhānām vraṇinām api | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.34x"><label>1.45.34x</label>
       jñeyaḥ pathyatamaś cāpi mudgayūṣaḥ kṛtākṛtaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.b"><label>1.45.b</label>
       prīṇanaḥ prāṇajananaḥ śvāsakāsakṣayāpaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       vātahantāśramaharo hṛdyo māṃsarasaḥ smṛtaḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.c"><label>1.45.c</label>
       khalāḥ khalayavāgvaś ca rāgaṣāḍavaṣaṭṭakāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       evam ādīni cānyāni kriyante vaidyavākyataḥ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.d"><label>1.45.d</label>
       yad ākāraṇam āsādya bhoktṝṇāṃ cchandato 'pi vā |
      <caesura/>
       anekadravyayonitvāc chāstra-tas tām vinirddiśet || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.31"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.36"/>
     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.37"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.43cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.43cd</label>
       snigdhaṃ svādu rasaṃ hṛdyaṃ vṛṃhaṇam valavattaraṃ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.44ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.44ab</label>
       vṛṣyam pittapipāsāghnaṃ nālikerodakaṅ guruḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.44cd"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.47ab"><label>1.45.47ab</label>
       gavyamājan tathā coṣṭramāvikaṃ māhiṣañ ca yat | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.47cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.47cd</label>
       aśvāyāś caiva nāryāś ca nāgyoś caiva tu yat smṛtaṃ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.48ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.48ab</label>
       tatvanekauṣadhirasaḥ prasādakṣīratāṅ gataḥ | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.48cd"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.48ef"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.48ef</label>
       sarvvaprāṇabhṛtān tasmāt sātmyaṃ kṣīramiho-cyate || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.49"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.49</label>
       gavyan tu śitasnigdhamadhuram avidāhi vātapittaśleṣmaśoṇitamānaseṣu vikāreṣv
      aviruddhaṃ |
      jīrṇṇajvarakāsaśophakṣayaraktapittagulmodaramūrcchābhramamadapipāsāpāṇḍurogārśa
      udāvarttātīsārayonirogagarbhbhāsrāvaśramaklamaharam valyaṃ vṛṣyaṃ rasāyanaṃ medhyaṃ
      vyājīkakaraṇaṃ sandhānam āsthāpanam āyuṣyam vamanam virecanañ ceti || thāpanaṃ
      tulyaguṇatvāc caujaso vardhanaṃ bālavṛddhakṣatakṣīṇānāṃ kṣudvyavāyavyāyām
      akarśitānāṃ ca pathyatamam || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.50ab"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.50cd"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.51ab"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.214"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.214</label>
       dhānyāmlan dhānyayonitvāt prāṇadhāraṇam amlatvād vātaghnam vidāhitvāt pittakaraṃ
      kaphaghnam va hiḥ śītaṃ guruvipākaṃ hṛdyatvāt tṛṣṇāpanayanaṃ rucijananaṃ
      samudrāntasaṃśritānāṃ ca janānām paraṃ sātmyaṃ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.204cd"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.204cd</label>
       tasyānekaprakārasya madyasya rasavīryataḥ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.205"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.205</label>
       saukṣmyādauṣṇāc ca taikṣṇyāc ca vikāsitvāc ca vahninā |
      <caesura/>
       sametya hṛdaye prāpya dhamanīm ūrdhvam āgataṃ |
      <caesura/>
       vicālyendriyacetāṃsi vīryam madayate</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.206"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.206</label>
       cireṇa ślaiṣmike puṃsi pānato jāyate madaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       vātike jāyate tīkṣṇaḥ paittike śīghram eva tu ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.207"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.207</label>
       sāndhike saucadākṣiṇyaharṣamaṇḍanavat sthitaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       vātike jāyate tīkṣṇaḥ paittike śīghram eva tu ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.208"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.208</label>
       rājase duḥkhaśīlatvam ātmatyāgaṃ susāhasaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       kalahaṃ sānavasthānaṃ karoti puruṣe madaḥ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.209"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.209</label>
       asaucanidrāmātsaryam agamyagamanaḥ sadā |
      <caesura/>
       asatyabhāṣaṇañ cāpi kuryād vai tāmase madaḥ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.215"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.216"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.217v"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.217"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.218v"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.218"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.218</label>
       tīkṣṇaṃ kaṭukaṃ mūtraṃ lavaṇānurasaṃ laghuḥ |
      <caesura/>
       śodhanaṃ kaphavātaghnaṃ śṛṇu tasya viśeṣaṇaṃ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.219"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.220"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.221"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.222"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.222</label>
       ānāhaśophagulmeṣu pāṇḍuroge tu māhiṣaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       śophaghnamājamaurabhraṃ kāsaśvāsaviṣāpahaṃ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.223"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.224"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.225"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.225</label>
       āśvaṅ kaphaharaṃ mūtraṃ krimidardruṣu śasyate ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.226"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.226</label>
       tīkṣṇaṃ kṣāre kilāse ca nāgamūtram prayojayet |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.227"/>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.228"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.228</label>
       arśoghnaṅ kārabhaṃ mūtram mānuṣantu viṣāpahaṃ ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.45.229"><label>1931 ed. 1.45.229</label>
       dravadravyāṇi sarvvāṇi kīrttitāni samāsataḥ |
      <caesura/>
       deśakālavibhāgajño nṛpateḥ karttum arhati</l>

    <div n="46" type="adhyāya">
     <head xml:lang="en">[Adhyāya 46, draft based on MS H]</head>




     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.1"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.1</label>
       athāto 'nnapānavidhim vyākhyāsyāmaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.2"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.2</label>
     </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.3"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.3</label>
       dhanvantarim abhivādya suśruta uvāca || bhagavan prāgabhihitam prāṇināṃ mūlam āhāro
      balavarṇṇaujasāñ ca saḥ ṣaṭsu raseṣv āyatto rasāḥ punar dravyāśrayiṇaḥ |
      dravyarasavīryavipākanimitte ca kṣayavṛddhī doṣāṇāṃ sātmyañ ca | brahmāder api ca
      lokasyāhāraḥ sthityutpattihetur āhārādevābhivṛddhir balam ārogyavarṇendriyaprasādaś
      ca | tathā hy āhāravaiṣampādasvāsthyan tasyāsitapītalīḍhakhāditasya
      nānādravyātmakasyānekavidhavikalpaprabhāvasya pṛthak pṛthak
      dravyarasavīryavipākakarmmecchāṃ jñātuṃ na hy anavabuddhadravyasvabhāvā bhiṣajo
      roganigrahaṅ karttuṃ samarthā ity āhārāyattāś ca prāṇino yasmāt tasmād
      annapānavidhim upadiśat tu me bhagavān ity uktaḥ provāca bhagavān dhanvantariḥ ||
      atha khalu vatsa suśruta || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.4"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.4</label>
       tatra
      lohitakaśālikalamakakarddamakapāṇḍukasugandhakasakunāhṛtakuṣmāṇḍakapuṇḍarīkamahāśāliśītabhīrukalodhraśūkadīrghaśūkakāñcanakahāyanakadūṣīmahākhyaprabhṛtayaḥ
      śālayaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.5"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.5</label>
       madhurā vīryataḥ śītā vipākā kaṭukāḥ smṛtāḥ | pittaghnālpānilakaphaḥ snigdhā
      vaddhālpavarccasaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.6"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.6</label>
       teṣāṃ lohitakaḥ śreṣṭho doṣaghnaḥ śukramūtralaḥ | cakṣuṣyo varṇṇavalakṛt svaryo
      hṛdyas tṛṣāpahaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.7"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.7</label>
       tasmād alpāntaraguṇāḥ kramaśaḥ śālayo pare || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.8"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.8</label>
       ṣaṣṭikakāṅgakamukundakapītakapramodakakālakāsanapuṣpakamahāsvetakamahāvrīhicūrṇṇakakuravakedāraprabhṛtayo
      vrīhayaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.9"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.9</label>
       rase pāke ca madhurāḥ pittānilaharāḥ smṛtāḥ | śālīnāṅguṇataś cāpi samānā
      vaddhavarccasaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.10"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.10</label>
       ṣaṣṭikaḥ pravaras teṣāṅ kaṣāyānuraso laghuḥ | mṛduḥ snigdhas tridoṣaghnaḥ
      sthairyakṛdvalavarddhanaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.11"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.11</label>
       rasato madhuragrāhī tulyo lohitaśālibhiḥ | śeṣās tv alpāntarās tv asmād vrīhayaḥ
      kramaśo guṇaiḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.12"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.12</label>
       kṛṣṇavrīhiśālāmukhalāvākṣajātumukhanandīmukhatvaritakakurkkuṭāṇḍakapārāvatakapāṭalāprabhṛ<cb
       n="2"/>tayo vrīhayaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.13"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.13</label>
       kaṣāyamadhurāḥ pāke madhurā vīryato 'himāḥ | alpābhiṣyandinastulyāḥ ṣaṣṭikair
      vvalavarddhanāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.14"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.14</label>
       kṛṣṇavrīhirvvarasteṣāṃ kaṣāyamadhuro laghuḥ | tasmād alpāntare guṇāḥ kramaśo
      vrīhayo 'pare || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.15"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.15</label>
       dagdhāyāmavanau jātāḥ śālayo laghupākinaḥ | kaṣāyā vaddhaviṇmūtrā rūkṣāḥ
      śleṣmāpakarṣaṇāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.16"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.16</label>
       sthalajāḥ kaphapittaghnāḥ kaṣāyāḥ kaṭukānvayāḥ | kiñcitsatiktamadhurāḥ
      pavanānalavarddhanāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.17"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.17</label>
       kaidārā madhurā vṛṣyā balyāḥ pittanivarhaṇāḥ | īṣatkaṣāyālpavalā guravaḥ
      kaphaśukralāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.18"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.18</label>
       ropyātiropyā laghavaḥ śīghrapākā guṇottarāḥ | avidāhino vātaharā valyā
      mūtravivardha-nāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.19"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.19</label>
       śālayaś chinnarūḍhā ye rūkṣā vaddhālpavarccasaḥ | tiktākaṣāyāḥ pittaghnā laghupākāḥ
      kaphāpahāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.20"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.20</label>
       vistareṇāyamuddiṣṭaḥ śālivarggo hitāhitaḥ | tadvat kudhāny amudgānām māṣādīnāñ ca
      vakṣyate || </l>





     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.21"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.21</label>
       koradūṣaśyāmākanīvāraśāntanuvarakoddālakapriyaṅgumadhūlikānandīmukhakuravindakasaka
      varūkatolaparṇṇāmukundakaveṇuyavaprabhṛtayaḥ kudhānyaviśeṣāḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.22"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.22</label>
       uṣṇāḥ kaṣāyamadhurā rūkṣāḥ kaṭuvipākinaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       śleṣmaghnā vātaniṣyandā vātapittaprakopanāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.23"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.23</label>
       kaṣāyamadhūrāḥ śītāsteṣāṃ pittasapāḥ smṛtāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       sakoradūṣaṇāmākonīraś caiva śāntanuḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.24"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.24</label>
       kṛṣṇāraktāś ca pītāś ca śvetāś caiva priyaṅgavaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       yathottaraṃ pradhānāḥ syūḥ snigdhāḥ kaphaharāḥ sarāḥ | </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.25"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.25</label>
       madhūlī madhurāḥ śītāḥ snigdhā nandīmukhī tathā |
      <caesura/>
       viśoṣī tatra bhūyiṣṭha varakaḥ samukundakaḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.26"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.26</label>
       rūkṣā veṇuyavā jñeyā vīryoṣṇā kaṭupākinaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       vaddhamūtraḥ kaphaharāḥ kaṣāyā vātakopanāḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.27"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.27</label>
       mudgavanamudgasūramukuṣṭhakalāyahareṇvāḍhakīsatīnā vaidalāḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.28"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.28</label>
       kaṣāyamadhurāḥ śītā kaṭupākā nilāpahāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       vaddhamūtrapurīṣāś ca pittaśleṣmaharās tathā || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.29"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.29</label>
       nātyarthavātalāsteṣām mudgādṛṣṭhi prasādanāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       pradhānā haritās tatra vanyā mudgasamāḥ smṛtāḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.30"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.30</label>
       vipāke madhurāḥ proktā masūrā vaddha varccasaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       maukuṣthakāḥ krimiharāḥ kalāyāḥ pracūrānilāḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.31"/>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.32"/>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.33"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.33</label>
       hareṇava satīnāś ca vijñeyābhinnavarccasaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       ṛte mudgam asūrābhyām anye cādhmānakārakāḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.34"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.34</label>
       māṣo gururbbhinnapurīṣamūtraḥ snigdho 'tha vṛṣyo madhuro 'nilaghnaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       santarppaṇaḥ stanyakaro viśeṣād valapradaḥ śukrakaphāvahaś ca || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.35"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.35</label>
       kaṣāyabhāvān na purīṣabhedī na mūtralo naiva lavāsa karttā |
      <caesura/>
       svādurvripāke madhuronasāndraḥ santarppaṇastanyarucipradaś ca || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.36"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.36</label>
       māṣaiḥ samānaṃ phalam ātmaguptam uktañ ca kākāṇḍuphalaṃ tathaiva |
      <caesura/>
       āraṇyamāṣā guṇataḥ pradiṣṭā rūkṣāḥ kaṣāyā avidāhinaś ca || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.37"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.37</label>
       uṣṇaḥ kulattho rasataḥ kaṣāyaḥ kaṭūrvvipāke kaphamārutaghnaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       śikrāśmarīgulmanisūdanaś ca sāṅgrāhikaḥ pīnasakāsahantā || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.38"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.38</label>
       ānāhamedo gudakīlahikkāśvāsāpahaḥ śoṇitapittakṛc ca |
      <caesura/>
       valāsa hantā nayanāmayaghno viśeṣato vanyakulattha uktaḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.39"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.39</label>
       īṣatkaṣāyo madhuraḥ satiktaḥ sāṃgrāhikaḥ pittakarās tathoṣṇaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       tilo vipake kaṭūko valiṣṭhaḥ snigdho vraṇo lepana pathyād uktaḥ || </l>


     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.40"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.40</label>
       dantyo 'gnimedhājanano 'lpamūtraḥ svaryo 'tha keśyo 'nilahā guruś ca |
      <caesura/>
       tileṣu sarvvaṣ eva sitaḥ pradhāno madhyaḥ sito hīnatarās tathānye || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.41"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.41</label>
       yavaxkaṣāyo madhuro himaś ca kaṭur vvipāke kaphapittahantā |
      <caesura/>
       vraṇeṣu pathyāstilavac ca nityaṃ pravṛddhamūtro bahuvātavarccāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.42"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.42</label>
       sthairyāgnimedhāsvaravarṇṇakṛc ca sapicchilaḥ sthūlavilekhanaś ca |
      <caesura/>
       medo 'nilastṛtṛraṇo 'tha rūkṣaḥ prasādanaḥ śoṇitapittayoś ca || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.43"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.43</label>
       ebhir gguṇair hīnataraiś ca kiñcid vidyād yavebhyo 'pi yavān aśeṣān |
      <caesura/>
       godhūma ukto madhuro guruś ca valyaḥ sthiraḥ śukravalapradaś ca || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.44"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.44</label>
       snigdho 'tha śīto 'nilapittahantā sandhānakṛc chleṣmakaraḥ saraś ca |
      <caesura/>
       rūkṣaḥ kaṣāyo viṣaśokhaśukravalāsadṛṣṭikṣayakṛdvidāhī || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.45"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.45</label>
       kaṭurvvipāke madhuraś ca simvaḥ prabhinnaviṇmārutapittalaś ca |
      <caesura/>
       śitāśitā pītakinaḥ kuvarṇṇā bhavanti ye 'nyekisarāś ca simvāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.46"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.46</label>
       yathoditas te guṇataḥ pradhānā jñeyās tathārddrā rasapākayoś ca |
      <caesura/>
       sahādvayaṃ mūlakapādikā ca kusiddhavallīprabhavāś ca śimbāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.47"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.47</label>
       jñeyā vipāke madhurā rase ca valapradāḥ pittanibarhaṇāś ca |
      <caesura/>
       vidāhavantaś ca bhṛśañ ca rūkṣā viṣṭabhya jīryanty anilapradāś ca || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.48"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.48</label>
       rucipradāś caiva sudurjjarāś ca sarvvāḥ smṛtā vaidalikāś ca śimbāḥ |
      <caesura/>
       kaṭur vvipāke madhurānilaghno vidāhibhāvādahitaḥ kusumbaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.49"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.49</label>
       uṣṇātasī svādurasānilaghnī pittolvaṇā syāt kaṭukā vipāke |
      <caesura/>
       pāke rase cāpi kaṭupradiṣṭa ssiddhārthakaḥ śoṇitapittakopī || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.49ef"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.49ef</label>
       snigdhoṣṇatiktaḥ kaphavātahantā tathā guṇaś cāśitasarṣapo pi || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.50"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.50</label>
       anārttavaṃ vyādhihatam aparyāgatam eva ca |
      <caesura/>
       abhūmijan navamvāpi na dhānyaṅ guṇavat smṛtaṃ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.51"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.51</label>
       navan dhānyam abhiṣyandi laghu samvat saroṣitaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       vidāhi guru viṣṭambhi virūḍham vātakopanaṃ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.52ab"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.52ab</label>
       śālyādeḥ sarṣapāntasya dvividhasyāsya bhāgaśaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       kālapramāṇasaṃskāro mātrā cāsmin parīkṣyate || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.53"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.53</label>
       ata ūrddhvam māṃsavarggam upadekṣyāmaḥ || tatra jaleśayā anūpā grāmyāḥ |
      kravyabhuja | ekasaphajāṅgalāś ceti | ṣaṇmāṃsavarggā bhavanti | teṣām uttarottarāḥ
      pradhānatamās te punar dvividhā ānūpajāṅgalāś ca | tatra jāṅgalavarggo 'ṣṭavidhaḥ |
      tatra jaṃghālā viṣkirāḥ pranudā guheśayāḥ prasahāḥ parṇṇamṛgāḥ | vileśayā grāmyāś
      ceti || teṣañ jaṅghālaviṣkirau pradhānatamau | </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.54"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.54</label>
       tatra jaṅghalā eṇahariṇarkuraṅga ṛṣya
      rālakṛtamālaśalabhaśvadaṃṣṭrīcāruṣkavṛṣatemṛgamātṛkāprabhṛtayaḥ kaṣāya madhurā
      laghavo vātapittaharāstīkṣṇā vastiviśodhanāḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.55"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.55</label>
       kaṣāyamadhurā hṛdyaḥ pittāsṛkkapharogahā |
      <caesura/>
       sāṅgrāhī rocano valyas teṣām eṇo jvarāpahaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.56"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.56</label>
       madhuro madhuraḥ pāke doṣaghno laghudīpanaḥ |
      <caesura/>
       śītalo vaddhaviṭmūtraḥ sugandhir hariṇaḥ smṛtaḥ || </l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.432"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.432</label>
       tatra pūrvvaśasya jā tānām vedarāmlaṃ | vaidalānān dhāmlaṃ | jāṅgalānān mṛgānān
      dhanvajānām pakṣiṇāñ ca pippalyāsavaḥ | viṣkirāṇāṃ kolavadarāsavaḥ | pratudānāṃ
      kṣīravṛksāsavaḥ | guhe śayānāṃ kharjjūranālikerāsavaḥ | sāmudrāṇām mātuluṅgāsavaḥ |
      kus̤māṇḍānām amlānām sārdvīkāsavaḥ | amlā amlānāṃ phalānāṃ padmotpalakandāsavaḥ |
      kaṣāyāṇāṃ dāḍimavetrāsavaḥ | madhurāṇāṃ trikaṭukayuktaḥ khadirāsavaḥ |
      tālaphalādīnāṃ dhānyāmlaṃ | kandānāṃ dūrvvānalavetrāsavaḥ | pippalyādīnāṃ
      svadaṃṣṭrāvasukāsavaḥ | cuccūprabhṛtīnāṃ lodhrāsavaḥ | kusumbhaśākasya tad eva |
      maṇḍūkaparṇyādīnām mahāpañcamūlyāsavaḥ | tālamastakādīnām amlaphalāsavaḥ |
      saindhavādīnāṃ surāsavam āranālan toyam vā || || bhavanti cātra ślokāḥ || </l>

       sa tu vyānena vikṣiptaḥ sarvvān dhātūn visarppati |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.527"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.527</label>
       kaphapittamalaḥ kheṣu svedaḥ syān nakharoma ca ||
      <caesura/>
       netraviṭ tvakṣu ca sneho dhātūnāṃ kramaśo malāḥ |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.528"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.528</label>
       divāvivuddhahṛdaye jāgrataḥ puṇḍarīkavat ||
      <caesura/>
       anupaklinna dhātvannam ajīrṇṇe 'pi hitaṃ niśi |</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.529"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.529</label>
       hṛdayaṃ līyate rātrau prasuptasya viśeṣataḥ ||
      <caesura/>
       samupaklinnadhātvannam ajīrṇṇe tvahitaṃ divā ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.530"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.530</label>
       imam vidhiṃ yo 'numatam mahāmuner mmaharṣimukhyasya paṭhet tu yatnataḥ |
      <caesura/>
       sa bhūmipāloya vidhātum auṣadham mahātmanāñ cārhati vaidyasattama iti || o ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.531"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.531</label>
       dravyajñānaṃ rasajñānam vasanañ ca virecanaṃ |
      <caesura/>
       dravadravyaparijñānam annapānena ṣaṭ smṛtaḥ || o ||</l>

     <l xml:id="SS.1.46.532"><label>1931 ed. 1.46.532</label>
       sūtrasthāne purā proktañ catvāriṃśat ṣaḍuttaraṃ |
      <caesura/>
       adhyāyāḥ kāśirājena pūrṇṇaṃ sarvvaṃ savistaraṃ ||</l>

     <p xml:id="SS.1.46.trailer">|| iti suśrute śalyatantre sūtrasthānaṃ samāptaṃ ||
      ||</p>



    </div>


   </div>

  </body>
